
1a1(mdo 'grel): jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa bzhugs//
1b1(mdo 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ bo d+hi pA tha pra dI paM/ bod skad du/ byang chub lam gyi sgron ma/ byang chub sems dpa' 
1b2(mdo 'grel): 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dus gsum rgyal ba thams cad dag dang de'i chos dang/ /dge
1b3(mdo 'grel): 'dun rnams la gus pa chen pos phyag byas te/ slob ma bzang po byang chub 'od kyis bskul gyur pas/ /byang chub lam
1b4(mdo 'grel): gyi sgron ma rab tu gsal bar bya/ /chung ngu 'bring dang mchog gyur pas/ /skyes bu gsum du shes par bya/ /de dag mtshan nyid
2a1(mdo 'grel): rab gsal ba/ /so so'i dbye ba bri bar bya/ /gang gi thabs ni gang dag gis/ /'khor ba'i bde ba tsam dag la/ /rang
2a2(mdo 'grel): nyid don du gnyer byed pa/ /de ni skyes bu tha mar shes/ /srid pa'i bde la rgyab phyogs shing/ /sdig pa'i las las ldog bdag nyid/ /
2a3(mdo 'grel): gang zhig rang don tsam don gnyer/ /skyes bu de ni 'bring zhes bya/ /rang rgyud gtogs pa'i sdug bsngal gyis/ /gang zhig gzhan gyi sdug
2a4(mdo 'grel): bsngal kun/ /yang dag zad par kun nas 'dod/ /skyes bu de ni mchog yin no/ /sems can dam pa byang chub mchog /'dod par
2b1(mdo 'grel): gyur pa de dag la/ /bla ma rnams kyis bstan pa yi/ /yang dag thabs ni bshad par bya/ /rdzogs sangs bris sku la sogs dang/ /mchod rten dam pa mngon
2b2(mdo 'grel): phyogs nas/ /me tog bdug spos dngos po dag /ci 'byor pa yis mchod par bya/ /kun bzang spyod las gsungs pa yi/ /mchod pa rnam pa
2b3(mdo 'grel): bdun dag kyang/ /byang chub snying po'i mthar thug par/ /mi ldog pa yi sems dag gis/ /dkon mchog gsum la rab dad cing/ /pus mo'i lha
2b4(mdo 'grel): nga sar btsugs nas/ /thal mo sbyar ba byas nas ni/ /dang por skyabs 'gro lan gsum bya/ /de nas sems can thams cad la/ /byams pa'i sems
2b5(mdo 'grel): ni sngon 'gro bas/ /ngan song gsum dang skye sogs dang/ /'chi 'pho sogs kyis sdug bsngal ba'i/ /'gro ba ma lus la bltas te/ /sdug bsngal
3a1(mdo 'grel): gyis ni sdug bsngal ba/ /sdug bsngal sdug bsngal rgyu mtshan las/ /'gro ba thar par 'dod pa yis/ /ldog pa med par dam 'cha'
3a2(mdo 'grel): ba'i/ /byang chub sems ni bskyed par bya/ /de ltar smon pa'i sems dag ni/ /bskyed pa'i yon tan gang yin pa/ /de ni sdong po bkod pa yi/ /mdo
3a3(mdo 'grel): las byams pas rab tu bshad/ /de yis mdo klog pa 'am bla ma la mnyan te/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems kyi yon tan mdza' med pa/ /rnam par
3a4(mdo 'grel): shes par byas la de gnas rgyu mtshan du/ /de ltar yang dang yang du sems ni bskyed par bya/ /dpas sbyin gyis zhus mdo dag las/ /'di yi bsod
3a5(mdo 'grel): nams rab bstan pa/ /gang de tshig bcad gsum tsam du/ /mdor bsdus 'dir ni bri bar bya/ /byang chub sems kyi bsod nams gang/ /de la gal
3b1(mdo 'grel): te gzugs mchis na/ /nam mkha' i khams ni kun gang ste/ /de ni de bas lhag par 'gyur/ /gang+gA'i bye ma'i grangs snyed kyi/ /sangs rgyas zhing rnams mi gang gis/ /rin chen dag gis kun bkang ste/ /'jig rten
3b2(mdo 'grel): mgon la phul ba bas/ /gang gis thal mo sbyar bgyi ste/ /byang chub tu ni sems btud na/ /mchod pa 'di ni khyad par 'phags/ /de la mdza' ni ma mchis so/ /byang chub smon pa'i sems dag bskyed nas ni//
3b3(mdo 'grel): 'bad pa mang pos kun tu spel bya zhing/ /'di ni skye ba gzhan duAng dran don du/ /ji skad bshad pa'i bslab pa'ang yongs su bsrung/ /'jug sems bdag nyid sdom pa ma gtogs par/ /yang dag smon
3b4(mdo 'grel): pa 'phel bar 'gyur ma yin/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub smon pa 'phel 'dod pas/ /de phyir 'bad pas 'di ni nges par blang/ /so sor thar ba ris bdun gyi/ /rtag tu sdom gzhan ldan pa dag /byang chub
3b5(mdo 'grel): sems dpa' i sdom pa yi/ /skal pa yod kyi gzhan du min/ /so sor thar pa ris bdun du/ /de bzhin gshegs pas bshad pa la/ /tshangs spyod dpal ni mchog yin te/ /
3b6(mdo 'grel): dge slong sdom pa dag tu bzheng/ /byang chub sems dpa' i sa dag gis/ /tshul khrims le'ur gsungs cho ga yis/ /yang dag mtshan nyid len pa yi/ /bla ma bzang las sdom pa 
4a1(mdo 'grel): blangs/ /sdom pa'i cho ga la mkhas dang/ /bdag nyid gang zhig sdom la gnas/ /sdom pa 'bogs bzod snying rjer ldan/ /bla ma bzang por shes par bya/ /de
4a2(mdo 'grel): la 'bad pas 'di 'dra ba'i/ /gal te bla ma ma rnyed na/ /de la gzhan sngo ma nod pa yi/ /cho ga yang dag bshad par bya/ /de la sngon tshe 'jam pa'i dpal/ /am+ba rA dza ra gyur pa yis/ /
4a3(mdo 'grel): ji ltar byang chub thugs bskyed pa/ /'jam dpal gyi ni sangs rgyas zhing/ /rgyan gyi mdo las bshad pa ltar/ /de bzhin 'dir ni rab gsal bri/ /mgon po rnams kyi spyan snga ru/ /
4a4(mdo 'grel): rdzogs pa'i byang chub sems bskyed cing/ /'gro ba thams cad 'gron du gnyer/ /de dga' khor ba las bsgral lo/ /gnod sems khro ba'i sems nyid dang/ /ser sna dang ni phrag
4a5(mdo 'grel): dog nyid/ /deng nas bzung nas byang chub mchog /thob kyi bar du mi bya'o/ /tshangs par spyod pa spyang bya zhing/ /sdig dang 'dod pa spang bar bya/ /tshul khrims sdom pa la dga' 
4a6(mdo 'grel): pas/ /sangs rgyas rjes su bslab par bya/ /bdag nyid myur ba'i tshul gyis ni/ byang chub thob par mi spro zhing/ /sems can gcig gi rgyu yis ni/ /phyi
4b1(mdo 'grel): ma'i mu mthar gnas par bgyi/ /tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i/ /zhing dag rnam par sbyang bar bya/ /ming nas bzung ba byas pa dang/ /phyogs bcu dag tu rnam par gnas/ /bdag gis lus dang ngag gi las/ /
4b2(mdo 'grel): thams cad du ni dag par bya/ /yid kyi las kyang dag bya ste/ /mi dge'i las rnams mi bya'o/ /rang gi lus ngag sems ni rnam dag rgyu/ /'jug pa'i sems kyi bdag nyid sdom gnas pas/ /tshul khrims bslab pa gsum la legs bslabs pas/ /tshul khrims bslab
4b3(mdo 'grel): pa gsum la gus cher 'gyur/ /de bas rnam dag rdzogs byang chub/ /sems dpa' i sdom pa'i sdom dag ni/ /'bad pas byas pas rdzogs byang chub/ /tshogs ni yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur/ /bsod nams ye shes rang bzhin gyis/ /tshogs ni yongs su rdzogs pa yi/ /rgyu ni
4b4(mdo 'grel): sangs rgyas thams cad dag /mngos shes bskyed pa nyid du bzheng/ /ji ltar 'dab gshog ma skyes pa'i/ /bya ni mkhar la 'phur mi nus/ /de bzhin mngon shes stobs bral bas/ /sems can don byed nus ma yin/ /mngon shes ldan pa'i nyin mtshan gyis/ /bsod nams
4b5(mdo 'grel): dag ni gang yin te/ /mngon shes dag dang bral gyur la/ /skye ba brgyar yang yod ma yin/ /myur du rdzogs pa'i byang chub tshogs/ /yongs su rdzogs par 'dod gyur pa/ /des ni 'bad bya mngon shes dag /'grub par 'gyur gyis le los min/ zhi gnas grub pa ma yin pas//
4b6(mdo 'grel): mngon shes 'byung bar mi 'gyur bas/ /de phyir zhi gnas bsgrub ba'i phyir/ /yang dang yang du 'bad par bya/ /zhi gnas yan lag rnam nyams pas/ /rab tu 'bad de bsgom byas kyang/ /lo ni stong phrag dag gis kyang/ /ting 'dzin 'grub par mi 'gyur ro/ /de phyir ting 'dzin tshogs
4b7(mdo 'grel): le'u las/ /gsungs pa'i yan lag la legs gnas/ /dmigs pa gang rung cig dag la/ /yid ni dge la bzhag par bya/ /rnal 'byor zhi gnas grub gyur pa/ mngon shes dag kyang 'grub par 'gyur/ /shes rab pha rol phyin sbyor dang/ brar pas sgrib? bzang mi 'gyur/ /de phyir
5a1(mdo 'grel): nyon mongs shes bya yis/ /sgrib pa ma lus spang ba'i phyir/ /shes rab pha rol phyin rnal 'byor/ /rtag tu thobs bcas bsgom par bya/ /thabs dang bral ba'i shes rab dang/ shes rab bral ba'i thabs dag kyang/ /gang phyir 'ching ba zhes gsungs
5a2(mdo 'grel): pa/ /de phyir gnyis ka spang mi bya/ /shes rab gang dang thabs gang zhes/ the tshom dag ni spang bya'i phyir/ /thabs rnams dang ni shes rab kyi/ /yang dag dbye ba gsal bar bya/ /shes rab pha rol tu phyin spangs pa'i/ /sbyin pa'i pha rol phyin la sogs/ /dge ba'i tshogs rnams thams
5a3(mdo 'grel): cad dag /rgyal po rnams kyis thabs su bshad/ /thabs bsgoms dbang gis bdag gis bdag nyid kyi/ /gang zhig shes rab rnam bsgom pa/ des ni byang chub myur dung thob/ /bdag med gcig pu bsgoms pas min/ /phung po khams dang skye mched rnams/ /skye ba med par rtogs gyur pa'i/ rang
5a4(mdo 'grel): bzhin stong nyid shes pa ni/ shes rab ces ni yongs su bshad/ yod pa skye ba rigs min te/ /med pa'ang nam mkha' i me tog bzhin/ /nyes pa gnyis kar thal 'gyur phyir/ /gnyis ka dag kyang 'byung ba min/ /dngos po rang las mi skye zhing/ /gzhin dang gnyis ka las kyang min/ /rgyu
5a5(mdo 'grel): med las co? nai? de yi phyir/ /ngo bo nyid kyi rang bzhin med/ /yang na chas rnams thams cad dag /gcig dang du mas rnams dpyad na/ /ngo bo nyid ni dmigs pas/ /rang bzhin med pa nyid du ngas/ /stong nyid bdun cu'i rigs pa dang/ /dbu ma rtsa ba sogs las kyang/ /dngos po rnams kyi rang
5a6(mdo 'grel): bzhin gyis/ /stong pa nyid ni grub bshad pa/ /gang phyir gzhung ni mangs 'gyur bas/ /de phyir 'dir ni ma spros la/ /grub pa'i grub mdza' tsam zhig tu/ /bsgom pa'i phyir ni rab tu bshad/ /de bas chos rnams ma lus pa'i/ /rab bzhin dag ni mi dmigs pas/ /bdag med pa
5a7(mdo 'grel): ni sgom gang yin/ /de nyid shes rang bsngom? pa yin/ /shes rab kyis ni chos rnams kun/ /gang gi rang bzhin ma mthong zhing/ /shes rab de nyid rig bshad pa/ rnam rtog med par de bsgom bya/ rnam rtog las byung srid pa 'di/ rnam par rtog pa'i bdag nyid de/ da
5b1(mdo 'grel): phyir ma lus rtog spangs pa/ /mya ngan 'das pa mchog yin no/ /de ltar yang ni bcom ldan gyis/ rnam rtog ma rig chen po ste/ /'khor ba'i rgya mtshor ltung bar byed/ rtog med ting 'dzin la gnas pas/ /nam mkha' bzhin du rtog med gsal/ zhes gsungs so/ rnam par mi rtog pa
5b2(mdo 'grel): la 'jug pa'i gzungs las kyang/ dam chos 'di la rgyal ba'i sras/ /rnam par mi rtog bsams gyur na/ rnam rtog bgrod ? ba rnams 'das te/ rim gyis ma rtog thob par 'gyur/ zhes gsungs so/ /lung dang rigs pa dag gis ni/ chos rnams thams cad skye med pa'i/ /rang bzhin med
5b3(mdo 'grel): ba nges byas nas/ rnam par rtog med bsgom par bya/ /de ltar de nyid bsgom byas nas/ /rim gyis dred sogs thob byas nas/ /rab dga' la sogs thob 'gyur te/ /sangs rgyas byang chub yun mi ring/ /sngags mthu nyid las grub pa yi/ zhi dang rgyas sogs las rnams kyis/ /bum
5b4(mdo 'grel): pa bzang grub la sogs pa/ /grub chen brgyad sogs stobs kyis kyang/ /bden pa yin ni byang chub tshogs/ /yongs su rdzogs par 'dod pa dang/ /bya ba spyod sogs rgyud gsungs pa'i/ /gal te bsang sngags spyod 'dod na/ /de tshe slob dpon dbang bskur phyir/ /bsnyen bkur rin chen
5b5(mdo 'grel): sogs sbyin dang/ bka' sgrub la sogs thams cad kyis/ bla ma dam pa mnyes par bya/ bla ma mnyes par 'gyur pa yis/ yongs su rdzogs slob dpon dbang bskur bas/ /sdig kun rnam dag bdag nyid ni/ /dngos grub sgrub pa'i skal ldan 'gyur/ /dang po sangs rgya brgyud chen las
5b6(mdo 'grel): rab tu 'bad pas bkag pa'i phyir/ /gsang ba shes rab dbang bskur ni/ /tshangs par spyod pas blang mi bya/ gal te dbang bskur de 'dzin na/ tshangs spyod dka' thub la gnas pas/ /bkag pa sbyang par gyur pa'i phyir/ dka' thub sdom pa de nyams te/ brtul zhugs can dag ma? ba
5b7(mdo 'grel): yi/ /ltung ba dag ni 'byung 'gyur zhing/ /de ni ngan song des ltung pas/ /drug? pa nan tsam yang 'od ma yin/ /rgyud kun nyan dang 'chad ga dang/ /sbyin sreg mchod sbyin sogs byed pa/ /slob dpon dbang bskang rnyed gyur cing/ /de nyid rig las nyes pa med/ gnas rtan mar me
6a1(mdo 'grel): mdzad dpal gyis/ /mdo sogs chos las bshad mthong ba/ /byang chub 'od kyis gsol btab nas/ /byang chub lam bshad mdor bsdus byas/ /byang chub lam gyi sgron ma slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa
6a2(mdo 'grel): rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang/ zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa chos 'di ni zhang zhung gi tho ling gtsug lag khang du mdzad do// //rgya gar skad du/ tsA rya saM gra ha pra dI baM/ bod skad du/ spyod pa bsdus
6a3(mdo 'grel): pa'i sgron ma/ 'jig rten dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang gis gsung gi 'od zer gyis/ /bdag sogs rmongs pa ma lus pa'i/ /snying gi pad+ma kha 'byed pa'i/ /dam pa'i skyes mchog de la 'dud/ /gsang sngags pha rol phyin pa la/ /brten nas byang chub bsgrub po zhes/
6a4(mdo 'grel): bla ma sangs rgyas gsung bas na/ /de don bdag gis bri bar bya/ /gsang sngags 'di ru brjod mi bya/ /pha rol phyin lugs spyod pa yi/ /byang chub sems pa'i spyod pa dang/ /mdo tsam bdag gis bshad par bya/ /sems skyed sngon du song ba yis/ /byang chub sems dpa' i
6a5(mdo 'grel): sdom pa blang/ /mdo sde ma lus kun blta zhing/ /bstan bcos mdza' dag mnyan par bya/ /lus dang ngag dang yid gsum gyis/ /ji skad bshad pa'i sdom pa rnams/ /ma nyams gtsang mar bsrungs byas la/ /tshul khrims rnam par dag par bya/ /zas kyi tshod kyang rig par
6a6(mdo 'grel): bya/ /dbang po rnams kyis sgo yang bsdam/ /nam gyi cha stod cha smad la/ /mi nyal rnal 'byor brtson par bya/ /khas? ma tho phra rab la 'ang/ /shin tu 'jigs pa bskyed par bya/ /mtshan mo cha gsum bgo bya ste/ /tha ma'i cha la ldang par bya/ /gdong la sogs pa bkru ba 'am/ /yang
6a7(mdo 'grel): na ma bkrus pa yang rung/ /bde ba'i stan la 'dus nas ni/ chos rnams chos nyid dran par bya/ /mtshan mas g.yengs sam ma nus na/ /langs la dngos po snang ba kun/ /sgyu ma lta bur nye bar brtag /bar skabs der yang dge sbyor ni/ /yan lag bdun pa rdzogs par bya/ /
6b1(mdo 'grel): smon lam shin tu rgya chen gdag /yang na sngar gyi sgom pa bsgom/ /de nas zas kyis dus dag tu/ /snying po med pa'i lus 'di yis/ /snying po dam pa btsal bya zhes/ /lus la gru yi blo bzhag la/ rgyags pa bskyed phyir mi bza' zhing/ /rol chags pas mi bza' o/ /zas la cha bzhir 'go
6b2(mdo 'grel): bya ste/ /dang po lha la bshos gtsang dbul/ /de rjes chos kyi srung ma la/ /gtor ma shin tu rgya chen gtang/ /rang gis zos shing 'thungs pa yi/ /lhag ma 'byung po kun la sbyin/ /bar skabs der yang sgrung rgyud dang/ /ngo mtshar can gyi gtam yang bya de nas langs la cung zhig
6b3(mdo 'grel): bcag /yang na rten la bskor ba bya/ /bzlas brjod glegs bam klag pa 'am/ /yang na bde gshegs gzugs brnyan bya/ /ji srid rdul ni ma byung ba/ /de srid skor ba ma yengs par/ /byas la smon lam rgya chen gdag /mdor na mgon po byams pa yis/ /bshad pa'i chos spyod bcu po rnams
6b4(mdo 'grel): yi ni rab tu ?g.yengs shing/ /sgyu ma lta bur dran pas sbyang/ /gal te yong na dge 'dun mchod/ /yang na byis pa'i ston mo bya/ /mgon med ngag la sbyin pa ni/ /rnal 'byor bsod nams tshogs su 'gyur/ /nyin mo'i bya ba rdzogs pa dang/ /mtshan mo'i cha ni dang po ru//
6b5(mdo 'grel): //chos nyid spros pa dang bral ba/ /shes pa'ang spros dang bral bar bzhag /mtshan mo'i gung la bab pa na/ /ldang dang snang ba'i 'du shes kyi/ /seng ge ji ltar nyal ba ltar/ /dge ba'i gnyid ni log par bya/ /spyir na mnyam gzhag sems brtan na/ /lus ngag dge ba gtsor
6b6(mdo 'grel): mi bya/ /yang na mnyam gzhag mi gsal na/ /'jig rten mthun 'jug bya ba'i phyir/ /lus ngag dge ba ci nus bya/ /'jig rten sems dang ma mthun na/ /'di ni bdag gis chos min zhes/ /bsam pa bzang po sngon btang la/ 'jig rten yul chos dri bar bya/ /nai pa la yis yul du ni//
6b7(mdo 'grel): rang gi grogs pos bskul nas byas/ /gsang sngags lugs la mi mos na/ /'di ltar mdzod cig s+thA bi ra/ /spyod pa bsdus pa'i sgron ma slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po paN+Di ta dI paM ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA
7a1(mdo 'grel): na de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus pa'o// //rgya gar skad du/ sa tyadwa yA ba tA ra/ bod skad du/ /bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa/ /thugs rje chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis chos bstan
7a2(mdo 'grel): pa/ bden pa gnyis la yang dag brten/ /'jig rten kun rdzob bden pa dang/ /de bzhin don dam bden pa'o/ /kun rdzob rnam pa gnyis su 'dod/ /log pa dang ni yang dag go /dang po gnyis te chu zla dang/ /grub mdza' ngan pa'i rtog pa'o/ /ma brtags gcig bu nyams dga' 
7a3(mdo 'grel): ba'i/ /skye ba dang ni 'jig pa'i chos/ /don byed nus dang ldan pa ni/ /yang dag kun rdzob yin par 'dod/ /dam pa'i don ni gcig nyid de/ /gzhan dag rnam pa gnyis su 'dod/ /cir yang ma grub chos nyid de/ /gnyis dang gsum sogs ga la 'gyur/ /bstan pa'i tshig gis sbyor pa
7a4(mdo 'grel): yis/ /skye med 'gag med sogs pas mtshon/ /don dam tha dad med tshul gyis/ /chos can med cing chos nyid med/ /stong pa nyid la tha dad ni/ /cung zad yod pa mi yin te/ /rtogs med tshul gyis rtogs pas na/ /stong nyid mthong zhes tha snyad gdags/ /ma mthong ba nyid de mthong bar/ /shin tu
7a5(mdo 'grel): zab pa'i mdo las gsungs/ /de la mthong dang mthong byed med/ /thog ma tha ma med zhi ba/ /dngos dang dngos med rnam par spangs/ /rnam par rtog med dmigs pa bral/ gnas pa med pa gnas med pa/ /'gro 'ong med cing dpe dang bral/ /brjod du med pa bltar med pa/ /'gyur ba med pa 'dus ma
7a6(mdo 'grel): byas/ rnal 'byor pa yis de rtogs na/ /nyon mongs shes bya'i sgrib pa spong/ /mngon sum dang ni rjes su dpag /sangs rgyas pa yis de gnyis bzung/ /gnyis pos stong nyid rtogs so zhes/ /tshu rol mthong ba'i rmongs pa smra/ /mu stegs nyan thos rnams kyis kyang/ /chos nyid rtogs par thal bar
7a7(mdo 'grel): 'gyur/ /rnam rigs pas lta smos ci dgos/ /dbum pa la mi mthun med/ /des na grub mdza' thams cad kyang/ /tshad mas 'jal phyir mthun par 'gyur/ /rtog ge thams cad mi mthun pas/ /tshad mas gzhal pa'i chos nyid kyang/ /mang po nyid du mi 'gyur ram/ /mngon sum rjes dpag dgos pa med?
7b1(mdo 'grel): mu stegs rgol ba bzlog pa'i phyir/ /mkhas pa rnams kyis byas pa yin/ /lung las kyang ni gsal po ru/ /rtog bcas rtog ma med pa yi/ /shes pa gnyis kyis mi rtogs shes/ /slob dpon mkhas pa b+ha bya gsung/ /stong nyid gang gis rtogs shes na/ /de bzhin gshegs pas lung bstan
7b2(mdo 'grel): cing/ chos nyid bden pa gzigs pa yi/ /klu sgrub slob ma zla grags yin/ /de las brgyud pa'i man ngag gis/ /chos nyid bden pa rtogs par 'gyur/ /chos kyi phung po brgyad khri dang/ /bzhi stong gsungs pa thams cad ni/ /chos nyid 'di la gzhol zhing 'bab/ /stong nyid rtogs pas grol 'gyur gyi/ /sgom
7b3(mdo 'grel): pa lhag ma de don yin/ /yang dag kun rdzob khyad bsad nas/ /stong pa nyid la goms byed na/ /kun rdzob rgyu 'bras dge sdig sogs/ /'jig rten pha rol bslus par 'gyur/ /cung zad thos pa la brten te/ /rnam par dben don zhi shes shing/ /mi gang bsod nams mi byed pa/ /skye bu tha shal de dag
7b4(mdo 'grel): brlag /stong pa nyid la blta nyes na/ /shes rab chung ldan phung bar 'gyur/ /slob dpon zla grags 'di skad du/ /thabs su gyur pa kun rdzob bden pa dang/ thabs las byung ba don dam bden pa dag /gnyis po'i dbye ba gang gis mi shes pa/ /de dag log par rtogs nas ngan 'gror 'gro//
7b5(mdo 'grel): tha snyad la ni ma brten par/ /dam pa'i don ni rtogs mi 'gyur/ /yang dag kun rdzob rnams kyi skas?/ /med par yang dag khang chen gyi/ /steng du 'gro bar byed pa ni/ /mkhas la rung ba ma yin no/ /kun rdzob ji ltar snang ba 'di ga? rigs pas brtags na 'ga' mi rnyed/ /ma rnyed pa nyid don dam
7b6(mdo 'grel): yin/ yi nas gnas pa'i chos nyid do/ /rgyu rkyen dag gis bskyed pas na/ /kun rdzob ji ltar snang ba grub/ /gal te grub par mi rung na/ /chu zla la sogs su yis bskyed/ /des na rgyu rkyen sna tshogs kyis/ /bskyed pas snang ba thams cad grub/ /rkyen rnams rgyun ni chad gyur na/ /kun rdzob
7b7(mdo 'grel): tu yang mi 'byung ngo/ /de ltar lta bas ma rmongs shing/ /spyod pa shin tu dag gyur na/ /gol ba'i lam du mi 'gro zhing/ /'og min gnas su 'gro bar 'gyur/ /tshe ni yun thung shes bya'i rnam pa mang/ tshe yi tshad kyang ji tsam mi shes pas/ /dad pa chu las 'o ma len pa ltar/ /rang gi 'dod
8a1(mdo 'grel): pa dang la blang bar gyis/ /tshu rol mthong ba'i rmongs pa dag gis ni/ /bden gnyis gtan la dbab par mi 'os kyang/ /bla ma rnams kyis gsung la brten nas ni/ /klu sgrub lugs kyi bdon gnyis bkod pa 'di/ /gser gling rgyal po'i dor
8a2(mdo 'grel): byas 'di la ni/ /gal te deng sang skye bo dang gyur kyang/ /legs par brtags la blangs pa nyid du bya'i/ /dad pa tsam dang gus pa tsam gyis min/ /gser gling rgyal po gu ru pha ma yis/ /dge slong de ba ma ti btang gyur nas/ /de yi dor byas bden gnyis la 'jug 'di//
8a3(mdo 'grel): deng sang mkhas pa rnams kyis brtags par rigs/ /bden pa gnyis la 'jug pa slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba rgya brtson 'grus seng ges bsgyur cing zhus te gtan
8a4(mdo 'grel): la phab pa'o// //rgya gar skad du/ ma d+hya mo pa de sha nA ma/ bod skad du/ dbu ma'i man ngag ces bya ba/ 'jig rten mgon po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang gi gsung gi 'od zer gyis/ /bdag sogs rmongs pa ma lus pa'i/ /snying gi pad+ma kha 'byed pa'i/ /dam pa'i skyes
8a5(mdo 'grel): mchog de la 'dud/ theg pa chen po dbu ma'i man ngag ni 'di yin te/ kun rdzob tu chos thams cad tshu rol mthong ba'i dong byas nas/ rgyu 'bras la sogs pa rnam par bzhag pa thams cad ji ltar snang ba bzhin du bden pa yin la/ don dam pa 'am yang dag par
8a6(mdo 'grel): na kun rdzob ji ltar snang ba de kho na gtan tshigs chen po rnams kyis gzhigs shing btsal na/ skra'i rtse mo brgyar gshags pa'i tshad tsam yang gzung du med do zhes nges par khong du chud par bya'o/ /stan bde ba la skyil mo krung bcas te 'dug la/ 'di ltar re zhig
8a7(mdo 'grel): dngos po ni gnyis te/ gzugs can dang/ gzugs can ma yin pa'o/ /de la gzugs can rnams ni rdul phra rab 'dus pa'i yin la/ de yang phyogs bcu'i dbye bas bye cing gzhigs na shin tu phra ba yang lus pa med cing shin tu snang ba yang med do/ /gzugs
8b1(mdo 'grel): can ma yin pa ni sems yin la/ de yang 'di ltar 'das pa'i sems ni 'gags shing zhig /ma 'ongs pa'i sems ni ma skyes shing ma byung/ da ltar gyi sems ni 'di ltar yang shin tu brtags dka' ste/ kha dog med cing dbyibs dang bral ba/ nam mkha' dang 'bra bas ma grub pa 'am/
8b2(mdo 'grel): yang na gcig dang du ma dang bral bas sam/ yang na ma skyes pas sam/ yang na de rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba la sogs pa rigs pa'i mtshon gyis dpyad cing gzhigs na ma grub par rtogs so/ /de ltar gnyis po ci'i ngo bor yang ma grub cing med tsam na so sor rtog pa'i shes rab de
8b3(mdo 'grel): nyid kyang ma grub ste/ dper na shing gnyis phan tshun drung bas me byung ba'i rkyen gyis shing gnyis po nyid tshig cing med pa'i rjes la gang gis sreg par byed pa'i me de nyid kyang rang zhi ba de bzhin du/ rang dang spyi'i mtshan nyid kyi chos thams cad med par grub tsam na shes rab nyid kyang snang
8b4(mdo 'grel): ba med cing 'od gsal ba ci'i ngo bor yang ma grub pas/ /bying ba dang rgod pa la sogs pa'i skyon du gyur pa thams cad bsal te/ bar skabs der shes pa cing yang mi rtog /cir yang mi 'dzin/ dran pa dang yid la byed pa thams cad spangs te/ ji srid du mtshan ma 'am/ rnam par
8b5(mdo 'grel): rtog pa'i dgra 'am/ chom rkun ma langs kyi bar du de lta bu la shes pa gnas par bya'o/ /gang gi tshe ldang bar 'dod na ngal? bus skyil mo krung bshigs la langs te/ sgyu ma lta bu'i yid kyi lus dang ngag dang yid kyis dge ba ci nus kyis bya'o/ /de ltar gus pa dang yun ring ba dang
8b6(mdo 'grel): rgyun mi chad par bsgrubs na skal pa dang ldan pa rnams kyis tshe 'di nyid la bden pa mthong bar 'gyur te/ chos thams cad nam mkha' i dkyil lta bu 'bad pa dang rtsol ba med cing rang gi ngang Tgis grub par mngon sum du byed do/ /de'i rjes la thob pas ni chos thams cad sgyu ma la
8b7(mdo 'grel): sogs par shes so/ /gang gis tshe rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin mngon du byas phan chad ni rjes las thob pa yang mi mnga' ste/ dus thams cad du mnyam par bzhag pa'o/ /de lta ma yin na byang chub sems dpa' dang khyad par ci yod ces bya ba la sogs pa'i rigs pa dang
9a1(mdo 'grel): lung 'dir mi brjod do/ /gzhan gyi don bskal pa grangs med par tshogs bsags pa dang smon lam btab pa'i mthus gdul bya rnams ji ltar 'dod pa bzhin du 'gyur ro/ /lung dang rigs pa shin tu mang mod kyi/ 'dir ma smros so/ /dbu
9a2(mdo 'grel): ma'i man ngag ces bya ba slob dpon dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang/ zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas lha sa 'phrul snang du bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ //rgya gar
9a3(mdo 'grel): skad du/ saM gra he garb+ha nA ma/ bod skad du/ snying po bsdu ba zhes bya ba/ thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /khams gsum sdug bsngal rgya mtsho che'i/ /dba' rlabs shin 'khrugs pa ni/ /dge dang mi dge la sogs pa'i/ /zag bcas las las nges par 'byung//
9a4(mdo 'grel): de dag chags sdang la sogs pa'i/ /nyon mongs rgyu yis bskyed pa ste/ /de dag 'byung ba'i rgyu nyid kyang/ /yid du 'ong dang mi 'ong sogs/ /gnyis su 'dzin pa 'di las byung/ /thams cad 'byung ba'i rgyu nyid ni/ /rtag dang khyab dang gcig pu sogs/ /dngos por 'dzin pa'i gdon
9a5(mdo 'grel): yin te/ /de bas skal ldan skyes bu ni/ /bdag gzhan grol ba don gnyer bas/ /rten cing 'brel 'byung la sogs pa'i/ /rigs pa gang la goms pa yis/ /dngos por 'dzin pa bzlog par bya/ /phyi nang chos rnams thams cad kun/ /mtshan ma thams cad dang bral ba'i//
9a6(mdo 'grel): nam mkha' lta bur shes bya las/ /dngos 'dzin gdon gyis brlams pa yi/ /'gro kun yul du byas nas ni/ /sdug bsngal rgya mtsho skems byed pa/ /snying rje chen po sngon 'gro bas/ /bdag gzhan don kun 'byung ba yin/ /rin chen byang chub sems bskyed bya/ /byang
9a7(mdo 'grel): chub spyod ba rlabs chen po/ /pha rol phyin drug la sogs la/ /mnyam gzhag langs pa'i sbyor ba yis/ /lam lnga rim gyis bgrod byas te/ /sgrib pa rnam gnyis bsal byas nas/ /tshogs gnyis yongs su rdzogs pa las/ /'bras bu sku gsum bsgrub bar bya sku
9b1(mdo 'grel): gsum 'byung ba'i mtshan nyid kyang/ /stong nyid nam mkha' lta bu las/ /bcol med thugs rje'i sprin 'byung zhing/ /sku gnyis bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun gyis/ /khams gsum tha ba'i rgyud brlan te/ /byang chub snying po'i sa bon las/ /dge ba'i lo tog smin bar 'gyur/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi
9b2(mdo 'grel): snying po de/ /'di ni snying po bsdus ba yin/ /tha ma'i dus su gyur bas na/ /tshe thung nad mang longs spyod dman/ /rkyen ngan bar chad mang ba yis/ /yun rig gnas ba'i mthu med pas/ /tshig rjes bcad par mi nus kyis/ /bshes gnyen dam pa bsten byas te/ /shin tu brtson pa'i
9b3(mdo 'grel): sems ldan bas/ /g.yangs rab tu dran bya ste/ /bdag gzhan grol bar bya ba'i phyir/ /snying po myur du bsdu ba yin/ /brtse bas 'di byas bsod nams kyis/ /skal ngan sems can thams cad kyang/ /byang chub sems dang ldan gyur nas/ /snying po myur du sdud par shog /snying po bsdu ba
9b4(mdo 'grel): zhes bya ba slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //paN+Di ta de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims 'byung gnas zhi bas bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o// //rgya gar skad du/ h+ri da ya ni kri ba ta nA ma /
9b5(mdo 'grel): bod skad du/ snying po nges par bsdu ba zhes bya ba/ /dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mngon mtho nges par 'byung ster ba/ /dkon mchog gsum la gus btud nas/ /'khor ba'i 'jigs pa sel ba yi/ /snying po bsdu ba bshad bar bya/ /'khor ba'i mtshan nyid sdug bsngal dang/
9b6(mdo 'grel): las dang nyon mongs rnam rtogs te/ /de dag rgyu 'bras go rim can/ /'khor ba bsdus nas bstan ba yin/ /thar pa'i mtshan nyid byang chub ste/ /shes rab thabs dang spyod pa dang/ /lam lnga dang ni tshogs gnyis las/ /mya ngan 'das pa'i sku gsum 'byung/ /de yang rgyu 'bras go rim
9b7(mdo 'grel): can/ /thar pa bsdus nas bstan pa'o/ /khams gsum sdug bsngal rgya mtsho che/ /dpa' rlabs shin tu 'khrugs pa ni/ /dge dang mi dge la sogs pa'i/ /zag bcas las las nges par 'byung/ /de dag gti mug chags sdang sogs/ /nyon mongs rgyu yis bskyed pa ste/ /yid 'ong
10a1(mdo 'grel): mi 'ong la sogs pa'i/ /gnyis su 'dzin pa nyid las byung/ /thams cad 'byung ba'i rgyu nyid ni/ /nga dang bdag tu 'dzin las byung/ /gzhan yang 'byung ba'i rgyu nyid ni/ /rtag dang gcig pu khyab la sogs/ dngos por 'dzin pa'i gdon yin te/ /shes rab ldan pas spang
10a2(mdo 'grel): bar bya/ /de bas skal ldan skyes bu ni/ /bdag gzhan ma lus grol bya'i phyir/ /mi slu ba yi lus ngag dang/ /rten cing 'brel 'byung la sogs pa'i/ /rigs pa gang la goms pa yis/ /dngos por 'dzin pa'i gdon chen po/ /ma lus par ni bzlog par bya/ /'di ltar phyi nang chos rnams
10a3(mdo 'grel): ni/ mtshan ma kun bral rang bzhin ni/ /nam mkha' lta bur shes byas la/ /rtag tu goms par bsgrub par bya/ /'khor ba thog ma med pa nas/ /dngos 'dzin gdon gyis brlams pa yis/ /'gro kun yul du byas nas ni/ /thams cad rjes su 'dzin pa yi/ /byams chen tshad med sngon 'gro
10a4(mdo 'grel): bas/ /sdug bsngal rgya mtsho skems byed pa'i/ /snying rje chen po tshad med pas/ /bdag dang gzhan don 'grub pa yis byang chub sems ni rin po che/ /yang dag bstan pa bskyed par bya/ /bdag gzhan 'byor pa bcu ldan bas/ /'khor ba'i chos las yid 'byung bya/ /'jigs pa kun
10a5(mdo 'grel): las skyong ba yi/ /skyabs gsum po dang ldan pa des/ /so sor thar la legs gnas bya/ /tshul khrims bzang po dang ldan cing/ /theg chen rigs yod skyes bu des/ /'gro ba skyabs med bskyab pa'i phyir/ /skyabs su 'gro ba sngon 'gro bas/ /smon pa'i sems ni bskyed par bya/ /lhag
10a6(mdo 'grel): pa'i bsam ba dang ldan pas/ 'jug pa'i sems ni bskyed byas pas/ /sngar gyi smon pa'i sems de nyid/ /rgya cher rab tu 'phel bar 'gyur/ /byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa ni/ /rlabs chen pha rol phyin drug sogs/ /mnyam gzhag langs pa'i rnal 'byor gyis/ /tshogs kyi
10a7(mdo 'grel): lam 'di bstan par grub/ /lam lnga rim gyis bgrod byas te/ /sgrib pa gnyis ni gsal byas nas/ /'di ltar tshogs gnyis rdzogs byas te/ /'bras bu sku gsum 'grub par bya/ /sku gsum bsgrubs pa'i mtshan nyid kyang/ /chos sku nam mkha' lta bu las/ /rtsol med thugs
10b1(mdo 'grel): rjes sprin byung bas/ /sku gnyis bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun gyis/ /khams gsum tha ba'i rgyud brlan te/ /byang chub snying po'i sa bon las/ /dge ba'i lo tog smin par 'gyur/ /dus gsum sangs rgyas kyis gsungs pa'i/ /snying po 'dir ni bsdus pa yin/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal spong 'dod na/ /de
10b2(mdo 'grel): la brtson 'grus 'bad par bya/ /rtsod pa'i dus kyi tha ma la/ /tshe thung nad mang yongs spyod dman/ /rkyen ngan bar chad mang ba yis/ /yun ring gnas pa'i mthu med pas/ /tshig rjes bcad par mi nus kyis/ /rigs la gnas pa'i gang zag des/ /bshes gnyen dam pa bstan byas la/ /shin tu
10b3(mdo 'grel): brtson ba'i sems kyis ni/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal dran byas la/ /bdag gzhan grol bar bya ba'i phyir/ /snying po myur du bsdu bar bya/ /brtse bas 'di byas dge ba yis/ /skal ldan sems can ma lus kun/ /byang chub sems kyis rgyud brlan te/ /snying po myur du sdud par shog /snying
10b4(mdo 'grel): po nges par bsdu ba zhes bya ba slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas dbus kyi snye thang gtsug lag khang du mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po chen po de nyid dang/ zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur cing zhus
10b5(mdo 'grel): te gtan la phab pa'o// //*/ /rgya gar skad du/ bo d+hi satwa ma N+yA ba li/ /bod skad du/ byang chub sems dpa' i nor bu'i phreng ba/ /thugs rje chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dad pa'i lha la phyag 'tshal lo/ /the tshom thams cad rnam spangs shing/ /sgrub la nan tan gces su
10b6(mdo 'grel): bya/ /gnyid rmugs le lo spang bya zhing/ /rtag tu brtson 'grus 'bad pa bya/ /dran dang shes bzhin bag yod pas/ /dbang po'i sgo rnams rtag tu bsrung/ /nyin mtshan dus gsum yang dang yang/ /sems kyis rgyud la rtag par bya/ /bdag gi nyes pa bsgrag bya zhing/ /gzhan gyi 'khrul pa btsal
10b7(mdo 'grel): mi bya/ /gzhan gyi yon tan bsgrag bya zhing/ /bdag gi yon tan sba bar bya/ /rnyed dang bkur sti spang bya zhing/ /khang grags rtag tu spang bar bya/ /byams dang snying rje bsgom bya zhing/ /byang chub sems ni bsten par bya/ /mi dge bcu po spang bya zhing/ /rtag tu dad pa brtan par bya//
11a1(mdo 'grel): 'dod pa chung zhing chog shes dang/ /byas pa drin du gzo ba dang/ /khro dang nga rgyal gzhom bya zhing/ /dman pa'i sems dang ldan par bya/ /log pa'i 'tsho ba rnam spang zhing/ /chos kyi 'tsho bas 'tsho bar bya/ /zang zing thams cad rnam spang zhing/ 'phags
11a2(mdo 'grel): ba'i nor gyis brgyan bar bya/ /dad pa'i nor dang tshul khrims nor/ /khrel yod ngo tsha shes pa'i nor/ /thos pa'i nor dang gtong ba'i nor/ /shes rab nyid kyi nor bdun po/ /nor gyi rnam pa 'di dag ni/ /mi zad pa yi gter bdun te/ /mi ma yin la brjod mi bya/ /rtag tu 'du 'dzi spangs
11a3(mdo 'grel): bya zhing/ dgon pa la ni gnas par bya/ /'khyal pa'i tshig rnams spang bya zhing/ /ngag rnams rtag tu bsdam par bya/ /bla ma mkhan po mthong ba'i tshe/ /gus pas rim gro bskyed par bya/ /gang zag chos kyi mig can dang/ /las dang po yis sems can la/ /ston pa'i 'du shes
11a4(mdo 'grel): bskyed bar bya/ /sems can thams cad mthong ba'i tshe/ /pha ma bu tsha'i 'du shes bskyed/ /sdig pa'i grogs po spang bya zhing/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten par bya/ /sdang dang mi bda'i sa spang zhing/ /gang du bde bar 'gro bar bya/ /gang la chags pa spang bya zhing/ /chags pa
11a5(mdo 'grel): med bar gnas par bya/ /chags pas bde 'gro mi thob cing/ /thar pa'i srog kyang gcod par byed/ /gang du dge ba'i chos mthong ba/ /der ni rtag tu 'bad par bya/ /thog mar brtsams pa gang yin pa/ /dang po de nyid bsgrub bya ste/ /de lta na ni kun legs byas/ /gzhan du
11a6(mdo 'grel): gnyis ka 'grub mi 'gyur/ /rtag tu sdig la dga' bral bya/ /gang du mtho ba'i sems 'byung tshe/ /de tshe nga rgyal bcag bya zhing/ /bla ma'i gdams ngag dran par bya/ /zhum pa'i sems ni byung ba'i tshe/ /sems kyi gzengs ni bstod par bya/ /rtag tu stong nyid bsgom bar bya/ /
11a7(mdo 'grel): gang du chags sdang yul byung na/ /sgyu ma sprul pa bzhin du blta/ /mi snyan tshig rnams thos pa'i tshe/ /brag cha bzhin du blta bar bya/ lus la gnod pa byung ba'i tshe/ sngon gyi las su blta bar bya/ /bas mdza' dgon bar rab gnas shing/ /ri dags shi ba'i ro bzhin du/ /
11b1(mdo 'grel): bdag gis bdag gnyis spang bya zhing/ /chags pa med par gnas bar bya/ /rtag tu yi dam brtan bya zhing/ /le lo rnyog pa'i sems byung tshe/ /de tshe bdag la brngan bgrang zhing/ /brtul zhugs snying po dran par bya/ /gal te gzhan dag mthong ba'i tshe/ /zhi des gsod bor smra ba dang//
11b2(mdo 'grel): khro gnyer ngo 'dzum spangs bya zhing/ /rtag tu 'dzum bzhin gnas par bya/ /rtag tu gzhan dag mthong ba'i tshe/ /ser sna med cing sbyin la dga' / /rtag tu phrag dog spang bar bya/ /gzhan gyi sems ni bsrung ba'i phyir/ /rtsod pa thams cad spang bya zhing/ /rtag tu bzod dang ldan par
11b3(mdo 'grel): bya/ ngo dga' med cing gsar 'grogs med/ /rtag tu zungs ni thub par bya/ /gzhan la brnyas pa spang bya zhing/ /gus pa'i tshul gyis gnas par bya/ /gzhan la gdams ngag byed pa'i tshe/ /snying rje phan sems ldan par bya/ /chos la skur pa gdab mi bya/ /gang mos 'di la 'dun par bya//
11b4(mdo 'grel): chos spyod rnam bcu'i sgo nas ni/ /nyin mtshan med par 'bad par bya/ /mang po'i nang du dag la brtag /gcig pur 'dug na sems la brtag/ dus gsum dge rtsa ci bsags pa/ /bla med byang chub chen por bsngo/ /bsod nams sems can rnams la bdar/ /rtag tu yan lag bdun pa yi/ /
11b5(mdo 'grel): smon lam chen po gdab par bya/ /de ltar byas na bsod nams dang/ /tshogs chen gnyis kyang rdzogs 'gyur te/ /sgrib pa gnyis kyang zas par 'gyur/ /mi lus thob pa don yod pas/ /bla med byang chub thob par 'gyur/ /rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad
11b6(mdo 'grel): pa byang chub sems dpa' i nor bu'i phreng ba rdzogs so// // */ /byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams ngag tu byas pa/ /sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /nges par legs pa'i byang chub dang/ /mngon par mthong ba thob 'dod bas
11b7(mdo 'grel): dkon mchog gsum la lhar bzung nas/ /dang po snying rjes kun la blta/ /de nas byang chub sems bskyed de/ /thabs dang ldan pa'i spyod pa yis/ /rang gis sems nyid dang bor gdul/ /dang por rang nyid ma dul bar/ /gzhan dag gdul bar ji ltar nus/ /ji ltar 'dab gshog
12a1(mdo 'grel): mchang ba'i/ /bya yis mkha' la 'phur mi nus/ /de bzhin lta spyod med pa yin/ /gang zag ngag ni ji ltar grol/ /de phyir de gnyis 'grub ba'i phyir/ /dka' ba'i 'bad pa chen pos bya/ /dka' bas sbyang ba ma byas par/ /sla bas goms
12a2(mdo 'grel): par ji ltar 'gyur/ /go bgos khur khyer rgyal sras des/ /dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten byas te/ /shes rab gsum la gzhi bcas nas/ /go 'phang mchog tu 'gro ba yi/ /lta ba nyid la gtsor sbyangs te/ /tshul khrims gtsang ma'i gos gyon nas/ /sgrub la nan tan bcos
12a3(mdo 'grel): su bya/ /chos kyi rjes su bsgrub pa'i phyir/ /dus dang gnas skabs kun tu yang ba sbyor ba dngos gzhi rjes gsum gyis/ /las rnams dran pas zin bar bya/ /skyon spang legs bsgrub don yod bya/ /spyod lam don med du mi gnas/ /rtag tu rang gi yon tan sbyang/ /dge ba'i
12a4(mdo 'grel): phyogs kyi sbyor ba la/ /spro bya zhum dang sems mi gsad/ /nyes spong yon tan dge 'phel ba'i/ /grogs btsal mthun ba de sems zung/ /yon tan can la gus phyag bya/ /nyon mongs skyes grogs thabs kyi spang/ /mthon dman grogs kun dag la yang/ /chu las 'o ma
12a5(mdo 'grel): len pa bzhin/ /nyes ba dor la legs par blang/ /byas la drin gzo slar phan gdags/ /gzhan gyi sdig rkyen mi bya zhing/ /dge ba'i bar chad mi bya'o/ /mtho la phun tshogs phrag mdog med/ /grogs dang dman la brnyas thabs dang/ /khyad du bsad pa nyid mi bya/ /rang
12a6(mdo 'grel): skyon gzhan gyi yon tan bsgang/ /gzhan skyon mi gleng rang mi bstod/ /'di bas phyi ma gtsang gzung ste/ /byed dgu chos dang bstun te bya/ /'di yi zang zing rnam spangs te/ /'phags pa'i nor gyis lus brgyan bya/ /sdug bsngal dag la bder mi gzung/ /gnyid rmugs le
12a7(mdo 'grel): lo ga ler spangs te/ /nges par 'chi ba'i 'du shes bskyed/ /dge ba'i chung yang 'bad bas bsgrub/ /sdig pa chung yang rnam par spangs/ /chos kyi ched du ma gtogs bar/ /kha zas gos sogs don mi gter/ /'dod pa chung dang chog shes bya/ /'jig rten chos
12b1(mdo 'grel): brgyad rnam par spang/ /do dga' gzhog slongs sogs mi bya/ /rang la skyon yod mi tshor bar/ /gzhan gyi skyon la dpyad mi bya/ /smra dga' khas len dpa' byas nas/ /de bzhin mi sgrub spang bar bya/ /g.yo dang sgyu dag mi bya zhing/ /log pa'i 'tshog rnam par spang/ /
12b2(mdo 'grel): chos dang mthun pas bsgrub bar bya/ /nye du 'brel pa la sogs la/ /zhen pas chags par mi bya zhing/ /phyogs ris zhen phyogs med bar bya/ /gzhan la ri ba chung bar bya/ /mi dga' i las la mi bstod smad/ /dgos ba med pa'i 'du 'dzi spang/ /bre mo'i gtam la
12b3(mdo 'grel): dga' mi bya/ /zhen pas 'dod pa'i yid smon dgag /yon tan thong dang tshogs 'phel ba'i/ /las la zhum dang ngo tsha spang/ /nga rgyal khengs dang gnyen pos gzhom/ /zhe gdung kheng grags rnam par spang/ /dngos dang brgyud pas sems can kun/ /nyes du 'brel
12b4(mdo 'grel): bar gyur bas na/ /lus ngag yid gsum dri med pas/ /de dag kun la bu bzhin blta/ /snying rjes bzhin 'dzum gsod por smra/ /dga' ba'i mig gis kun la blta/ /'khor grogs mthon dman nye ring snyoms/ /bstod dang bkur stis mi dregs shing/ /smod
12b5(mdo 'grel): dang brnyas la zhe mi sdang/ /phongs pa rnams la snying rje yis/ /phan ni gdags ba nyid du bya/ /gang la chags pa spang bya ste/ /dman pa rnams la snying rje dang/ /phan pa'i bsam pas gdams ngag bya/ /sems can bsam pa tha dad pas/ /bya ba don chen brtags te bya//
12b6(mdo 'grel): thams cad mgu bar su yis nus/ /'on kyang 'gyod pa med pa yis/ /sdug bsngal khyad bsang bde ma chags/ /rang gi sems sbyang gzhan sems gzung/ /brnyas dang nyes pa byung la sogs/ /gnyen po las dang brdzun pas sbyang/ /de ltar blta zhing byang chub
12b7(mdo 'grel): kyi/ /spyod pa yid dam brtan par bya/ /mi lus rin chen chung mi gsan/ /nges bar 'chi ba ma long mi srid/ /brtson 'grus me bzhin drag du sbyong/ /mngon zhen bdag lta'i rtsa ba chod/ /dus gsum 'khor ba gnyen pos chom/ /phyin ci log gi g.yang sa dor/ /'khor ba'i rgyun
13a1(mdo 'grel): chod las chu skoms/ /ngan song gsum po sgo chod la/ /sdug bsngal gsum gyi nang zhi ste/ /mtho ris thar ba'i skas ? 'dzegs/ /sgrib pa gnyis sbyongs tshogs gnyis rdzogs/ /sku dang ye shes la thob sto/ /'bad ba med par gzhan don bsgrubs//
13a2(mdo 'grel): byang chub sems dpa' i spyod pa mdo tsam gdams ngag tu byas ba slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar skad du/ si sA ra ma na nirya Ni ka sya gI ti/ bod skad du/ 'khor ba las yid nges par 'byung bar byed pa
13a3(mdo 'grel): zhes bya ba'i glu/ /bla ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo /e ma'o/ /'du byed sdug bsngal 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal dang/ /sdug bsngal sdug bsngal la sogs brgya rtsa bcu/ /sdug bsngal kun las skyob par mdzad pa yi/ /sman pa'i
13a4(mdo 'grel): rgyal po de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /kye kye kwa ye grogs po dag /'khor ba'i rgyu ni nyon mongs pa dang las/ /nyon mongs khams gsum gnas na dgu bcu brgyad/ /zag pa chu bo sbyor ba nye bar len/ /rgyu dang yul dang sbyor ba'i stobs kyis byung/ /kye kye kwa ye grogs po
13a5(mdo 'grel): dag /sna tshogs 'di dag las las gyur/ /de yang nyon mongs stobs las byung/ /dge dang mi dge lung ma bstan/ /mthong la myong ba skyes nas myong/ /gzhan du myong dang me nges pa'i/ /dkar dang gnag dang 'dren ma'o/ /'khor ba'i las ni lci gang dang//
13a6(mdo 'grel): nye ba gang dang goms pa gang/ /sngon byas gang yin de las ni/ /snga ma snga ma rnam smin 'gyur/ /grogs dag soms shig thog ma med pa nas/ /ma rig la sogs bcu gcig rga shi'i mdza' / /yan lag bcu gnyis cha gsum zo chu'i tshul/ /nang gi rten 'brel yang
13a7(mdo 'grel): dang yang du 'khor/ /tshe rabs tshe rabs grangs med de dang der/ /skye dang rga dang na dang 'chi ba yi/ /sdug bsngal rnams kyis yang dang yang du gdungs/ /'khrul nas 'khor gyur 'khrul cing 'khor bar 'gyur/ /kyi hud/ srid pa'i lam gyis dub pa'i 'dron po
13b1(mdo 'grel): rnams/ /sdug bsngal bde bar mthong nas mi skyo bar/ /khyod yid de la rtag tu chags byed pa/ /phyugs dang khyad par med par bla ma gsung/ bla mas zin pa'i skye bo mkhas pa dag /skad cig skad cig 'gro ba lnga po kun/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal tsher ma zug 'dra
13b2(mdo 'grel): la/ /dus pa'i gting nas snying rjes su mi skye/ /las ngan dbang gis 'khor pa'i rgya mtsho 'dir/ /yang yang skye zhing yang yang rga dang na/ /yang yang 'chi 'gyur 'di ni mi sems par/ /yul la chags byed bdag gis ji ltar bya/ /kye kye kwa ye grogs po dag /
13b3(mdo 'grel): srid pa gsum nang gnas pa kun sdug bsngal/ /de yang mi yis sdug bsngal bdag gis mthong/ /mngal gyi sdug bsngal 'di lta bur gnas/ /nur nur mer mer gor gor nar nar bo/ /ltar ltar mkhrang dang rkang lag rim gyis rdzogs/ /nu zho mar gyis gso byed
13b4(mdo 'grel): cing/ /shin tu nyam chung gan rkyal nyal/ /byis pa dar ma lang tsho dang/ rgas pas slar yang byis par 'gyur/ /tshe ni mi rtag shin tu g.yo ba ste/ /yud tsam sdod pa'i mthu yang yod ma yin/ /bdag ni nges par 'chi 'gyur mi sems pa/ /grogs dag skyes bu
13b5(mdo 'grel): de ni ngo mtshar che/ /'khor ba'i skyon dang nyes dmigs mi shes pas/ /phyin ci log pa bzhi la gnas nas su/ /bdag ni nges par 'chi 'gyur mi sems par/ /yul la mngon zhen nyin mtshan don med 'das/ /dzam bu'i gling pa dus min 'chi ba ste/ /nges pa can yang zas par
13b6(mdo 'grel): 'gyur bas na/ /yang dang yang du ngas par 'chi 'o zhes/ /bsam par rigs so kwa ye bzhin bzang dag /sos ka me tog rgyas pa'i dus 'di 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zla ba gsal bas mtshon pa'i ston dus 'di 'byung zhes/ /skye bo thams cad dga' 'gyur bdag gi tshe 'di ni//
13b7(mdo 'grel): zas par 'gyur zhes shin tu ming gar 'gyur ba med/ /de ring 'di bya sang ni 'di bya de nas 'di dang 'di bya zhes/ /srid pa g.yo ba'i rang bzhin ma shes don med yid brtan tshol byed pa'i/ /skye dgu 'chi bdag gi ni chu srin khar ni gzhi zhugs pa ltar/ /bya ba mthar ma phyin bar yul gyi chu yi dpa' 
14a1(mdo 'grel): klong nang du lhung/ /'di ni sang bya'i 'di ni thang cig 'og tu bya/ /'di ni de'u re bya zhes skye bo sems pa na/ /gshin rje'i be con lag thogs zur gyis lta byed cing/ /mig rtsa dmar khros mar bas gad mo re snyam 'debs/ /rnal 'byor bstan bcos thams
14a2(mdo 'grel): cad dang/ sbyor ba du ma shes rab kyang/ /deng bya sang bya zhes smra zhing/ /bsam dang ldan par 'chi bar 'gyur/ /tshe ni gnod mang rlung gis btab 'dra yi/ /chu yi chu bur bas kyang mi rtag na/ /dbugs 'byung dbugs rdub gnyid kyis log pa las/ /sad khom gang lags de ni ngo mtshar
14a3(mdo 'grel): che/ /kye kye kwa ye grogs po dag /tshe ni yun thung shes bya'i rnam pa mang/ /tshe yi tshad kyang ji tsam mi shes pas/ /ngang pa chu las 'o ma len pa ltar/ /rang gi 'dod pa rang la blang bar gyis/ /kye kye kwa ye grogs po dag /'jig rten spyod pa dag la phar bltas na/ /byas pa
14a4(mdo 'grel): thams cad don med sdug bsngal rgyu/ /ci la bsams kyang phan par mi 'gyur bas/ /rang gi sems la lta ba goms par gyis/ /kye kye kwa ye grogs po dag /tshad ma bdun dang brda sprod rnam pa bzhi/ /mngon pa dang ni yo ga tsarya'i sa/ /mdo sde dang ni 'dul ba mngon pa dang//
14a5(mdo 'grel): gzhung du bkod pa ma lus thams cad kun/ /ma mthong ma mnyan ma bshad ma bris zhes/ /de la gdung ba mi bskyed bzhin bzang dag /bla ma'i man ngag ces bya bdud rtsi'i ro/ /gang gis sems mnyam 'jog pa de tsam zhig/ yongs su btsal gyi gzhung mang ci zhig dgos/
14a6(mdo 'grel): thams cad yid ni 'khrul par byed pa'i rgyu/ /'khor ba'i gnas 'di nges pa med pas na/ /pha ma la sogs pha mar ma nges pas/ /nye du 'brel ba dag la chags pa spang/ /dgra yang ma nges de la sdang ba spang/ /nad med lang tsho phun sum tshogs pa dang/ /'dod yon lnga la rang bzhin gyis chags spang/ /rnyad
14a7(mdo 'grel): pa dang ni bkur sti grags pa dang/ /rigs dang rus dang tshigs su bcad pa spang/ /slob ma yang slob chos kyi 'brel pa spang/ /kyai kwa ye grogs po dag/ 'jig rten stag sbrul me dang dug 'dra bar/ /bsams nas spangs te dben bar gnas par bya/ /bud med mtshan nyid
14b1(mdo 'grel): skyes pa'i mtshan nyid dang/ /sman dang glang chen brtag pa 'am gza' skar rtsis/ /mtshon cha brtag pa 'am rta dpyad rang bzo 'am/ /bstan bcos ngan pa slob dang klag pa spang/ /yul la mngon dga' i sems ni byung ba dang/ /rnam rtog de dag rnams ni byung ba na/ /bdag ni
14b2(mdo 'grel): nges par 'chi ba dran byas la/ /'og nas 'byung ba'i gnyen po rnams kyi bzlog/ rnam rtog mang ba dbugs bgrangs pa yis gzhi la/ /'dod chags sems byung rnam par rtog pa de/ /rang bzhin mi gtsang keng rus lta bas bzlog /zhe sdang la ni byams pa'i chu yis
14b3(mdo 'grel): gdang/ /gti mug la ni rten 'brel lam gyis so/ /mi gtsang ba dang byams pa rten 'brel gyi/ /man ngag bla ma'i zhal nas byung bzhin bya/ /'khor ba las yid nges par 'byung bar byed ba zhes bya ba'i glu slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyi zhal snga nas mdzad
14b4(mdo 'grel): pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang/ zhus chen gyi lo tsA ba rgya brtson seng ges bi kra ma sh+rI la'i gtsug lag khang du bsgyur pa'o// //slad nas bla ma de nyid dang/ lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bcos shing gtan la phab pa'o// //
14b5(mdo 'grel): *// /rgya gar skad du/ tsArya gI ti/ bod skad du/ spyod pa'i glu 'phags pa 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal rdo rje gdan la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gzugs brnyan ci 'dra 'gro ba srid pa de 'dra ste/ /rang gi ngo bo brtags na rang bzhin yod ma yin//
14b6(mdo 'grel): rang gi ngo bo gzugs brnyan 'dra shes ma skyes pas/ /kwa ye rmongs pa'i sems khyod mi shes ma byed cig /dri med mkha' dang rgyas pa'i nor bu me long la/ /de la gsal bar snang ba bdag dang 'gro ba kun/ /de ltar byis ba rang gi gzugs brnyan la 'khrul ltar//
14b7(mdo 'grel): bdag gzhan 'byed pa'i 'khrul pa la ni ci phyir gnas/ /gang gis gzugs brnyan la ni rtag par shes shing rtogs/ /de ni phyugs dang 'dra ste grib ma la rgol yin/ /dkyil 'khor 'khor lo bsgom pa brtan par bya ba ste/ /de nyid shes pa'i rnal 'byor pa
15a1(mdo 'grel): yis der mi gnas/ /mtshon bar bya ba mchog tu bde chen gces pa ste/ /dkyil 'khor de la bsdus te bstan par bya ba yin/ /khyed kyis brtags shing bskyed pa'i tshul ni gang yin pa/ /de la de nyid rang bzhin yin par ji ltar
15a2(mdo 'grel): sems/ /ji srid de nyid rang bzhin yongs su ma shes pa/ /de srid byang chub bla na med pa ji ltar 'grub/ /rnam rtog spros pa ma lus dngos po med pa ste/ /de dag mchog tu bde ba chen po'i rang bzhin yin/ /'jig rten chos brgyad dag la sems ni mnyam pa dang/ /
15a3(mdo 'grel): ting nge 'dzin gyi tshogs la gnas par 'gyur bar gyis/ /gnas na shin tu rnam par dag par 'gyur ba ste/ /spros pa'i spyod pa ma lus yongs su spong ba yin/ /rnam par rtog pa sna tshogs kyis ni dngos gang bskyed/ /de ni mchog tu rnam par dag pa'i rang
15a4(mdo 'grel): bzhin min/ /spros pa dang ni rnam rtog ma lus yong min pa/ /de ni de bzhin nyid de mchog tu rnam dag dngos/ /de bzhin nyid kyi ting 'dzin me che 'bar ba ste/ /nyon mongs sog ma ma lus sregs par byed pa yin/ /gang tshe 'jig rten yongs su shes par
15a5(mdo 'grel): gyur pa na/ /de tshe 'gro ba thams cad nam mkha' bzhin du 'gyur/ /'gro ba'i rang bzhin mkha' 'dra ba la mi 'khrul cing/ /rnam rtog rab rib kyis rmongs ldongs bar ma byed cig /'gro ba sngon chad ci 'dra phyis kyang de 'dra ste/ /snga phyi dag dang bar la khyad
15a6(mdo 'grel): par yod ma yin/ /rab rib can gyis ji ltar mkha' la skra mthong dang/ /rnam rtog rab rib 'jig rten mthong la khyad par med/ /rnam rtog rang bzhin mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rang bzhin du/ /brtags pa'i rang bzhin ma lus pa dag bsgom par gyis//
15a7(mdo 'grel): sdig pa'i rnam smin chom rkun 'jigs pa mthong ba yis/ /kwa ye tshul khrims nor chen bsrung phyir mel tshe byos/ /srid pa'i mtshan ring dag la gti mug gnyid log gis/ kwa ye sems ni bag med me byed mel tshe byos/ /nyi ma med na nyin mo yod pa min
15b1(mdo 'grel): pa ltar/ /tshul khrims nor dang bral la bsam gtan ga la yod/ /gnyid log pa yi khang bar chom rkun zhugs pa yis/ /kwa ye khyod kyi tshul khrims nor chen phrogs ser/ /skad cig tsam yang bya ba ngan la ma chags par/ /de nyid nyi ma ma shar bar du
15b2(mdo 'grel): mel tshe byos/ /ji srid de nyid nyi ma dag ni shar ba na/ /de srid srid pa nor bu bzhin du ci dga' spyod/ /bdag ni gang yin 'gro ba khyed rnams de yin te/ /rang gzhan 'byed pa'i nang gi gnod pa ma byed cig /rnam rtog nang gi gnod pa 'di ni gzhom bya ste/ /sbrul
15b3(mdo 'grel): gdug lta bu de ni bdud rtsi'i ros zhi bya/ /nang gi gnod pa sbrul gdug mgo mangs lta bu ste/ /'gro ba ma lus sna tshogs rtog par shes nas ni/ /de bzhin nyid du bdud rtsi chen po'i ro zhes bya/ /rnal 'byor chen po'i sems kyi ngal so'i gnas gang yin/ /bdud
15b4(mdo 'grel): rtsi chen po'i ro ni rtag tu btung byas na/ bde ba chen po'i mya ngan 'das mchog shes par 'gyur/ /gcer bu sbyin sreg byed pa bram ze ma yin zhing/ /ral pa 'dzin pa dang ni rigs dang rgyud kyis min/ /gang zhig lus dang ngag dang yid ni yongs dag na/ /de lta
15b5(mdo 'grel): bu ni bram ze yin par sangs rgyas gsungs/ /sdig pa bcu po gang yin pa ni spang bya zhing/ /dge ba bcu po yon tan stobs dang ldan par bya/ /dman pa'i rigs su skyes kyang 'di ni gang gi tshe/ /ma shi bar du chos ma yin par spyad mi bya/ /bzod pa'i chos 'dzin pa yi khra
15b6(mdo 'grel): ba las rgyal zhing/ /yul gyi bde ba 'dod pa ma lus spang bar bya/ /bde ba'i chos kyi mtsho la rtag tu khrus bya zhing/ /'dun pa'i skyon dang 'jigs dang gti mug bskyed mi bya/ /yang dang yang du keng rus bzhon pa la bzhon cing/ /rtag tu mi gtsang 'dzag pa rmongs
15b7(mdo 'grel): pas mtshor ram/ /'dod dang gti mug ngan 'gro'i lam ni spang bya zhing/ /kwa ye sems khyod rang gi dri ma bkru bar gyis/ /gus pas bla ma dam pa'i chu mig bsten bya zhing/ /gti mug chen po'i dri mas gang gos zad par bya/ /bla ma'i man ngag de nyid dri med chu yin pas/ /
16a1(mdo 'grel): de blangs nas ni rang nyid bkru bar shes par bya/ /sems khyod yongs su go bar gyis la rang la ni/ /yongs su blta zhing gti mug dri ma chen po sbyongs/ /mi ni gang zhig thub pa'i chos gtam mi mnyan pa/ /de ni chu dang nags kyi mi dang mnyam pa yin/ /
16a2(mdo 'grel): nges par 'jig rten ma 'ongs pa rol 'gro bas na/ /thub pa'i chos kyi gtam ni mnyan par bya ba yin/ /thub pa'i chos thos nas ni chos min gnas mi bya/ /mnar med 'gro la lus kyang gzung bar mi nus pas/ /chos thos nas ni chos kyi don bzhin gang sgom pa/ /
16a3(mdo 'grel): des ni bde bar mtho ris thar pa'i 'bras bu thob/ /gti mug mun nag dag la chos ni sgron ma ste/ /srid pa'i mtsho las sgrol bar byed pa'i gzings yin no/ /slob dpon chen po dpal mar me mdzad ye shes kyis mdzad pa'i tshul khrims kyi spyod pa glur blangs par rdzogs so//
16a4(mdo 'grel): paN+Di ta badzra Ni dang/ lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la bab pa'o// //rgya gar skad du/ d+harma d+hA tu sa ra gI ti/ bod skad du/ chos kyi dbyings su lta ba'i glu/ /thams cad mkhyen pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang zhig kun tu ma
16a5(mdo 'grel): shes na/ /srid pa gsum du rnam 'khor ba/ /sems can kun la nges gnas pa'i/ /chos kyi dbyings la phyag 'tshal nas/ /chos dbyings lta zhing gzhan min par/ /de dag rim bzhin brjod par bya/ /zab zhi spros bral de bzhin nyid/ /'od gsal 'dus ma byas pa gang/ /
16a6(mdo 'grel): ma skyes ma 'gags gzod nas dag/ rang bzhin mya ngan 'das pa yin/ chos dbyings mdza' dang dbus med pa/ /blo mig zhib mo rtog bral ba/ /bying rgod rab rib med pas blta/ /gang zhig 'khor ba'i rgyur gyur pa/ /de nyid sbyang ba byas pa las/ /dag pa de ni mya ngan 'das/ /chos
16a7(mdo 'grel): kyi sku yang de nyid do/ /ji ltar 'o ma dang 'dres pas/ /mar gyi snying po mi snang ba/ /de bzhin nyon mongs dang 'dres pas/ /chos kyi dbyings kyang mi mthong ngo/ /ji ltar 'o ma rnam sbyangs pas/ /mang gyi snying po dri med 'gyur/ /de bzhin nyon mongs rnam sbyangs pas/ /chos dbyings shin tu dri
16b1(mdo 'grel): med 'gyur/ /ji ltar mar me bum nang gnas/ /cung zhig snang bar mi 'gyur ba/ /de bzhin nyon mongs bum nang gnas/ /chos kyi dbyings kyang mi mthong ngo/ /phyogs ni gang dang gang dag nas/ /bum pa'i bu ga btong gyur pa/ /de dang de yis phyogs nyid nas/ /'od kyi rang bzhin 'byung bar 'gyur/ /gang
16b2(mdo 'grel): tshe ting 'dzin rdo rje yis/ /bum pa de nyid bcag gyur pa/ /de tshe de ni nam mkha' yi/ /mthar thug bar du snang bar byed/ /chos kyi dbyings ni skye ma yin/ /nam yang 'gag par 'gyur ba med/ /dus rnams kun tu nyon mongs med/ /thog ma bar mdza' dri ma bral/ /ji ltar rin chen bai DUrya/ /dus rnams kun du
16b3(mdo 'grel): 'od gsal yang/ /rdo yi nang na gnas gyur na/ /de yi 'od ni gsal ma yin/ /de bzhin nyon mongs kyis bsgribs pa'i/ /chos dbyings shin tu dri med pas/ /'khor bar 'od ni gsal ma yin/ /ji ltar spun pas g.yogs gyur pa/ /so ba 'bras nyid mi 'dod ltar/ /de bzhin nyon mongs kyis
16b4(mdo 'grel): g.yogs pas/ /de ni sangs rgyas shes mi brtag /ji ltar spun pa las grol na/ /'bras nyid snang bar 'gyur ba ltar/ /de bzhin nyon mongs las grol na/ /chos kyi sku nyid rab tu gsal/ /ji ltar sgrum ma'i lto na bu/ /yod kyang mthong ba ma yin pa/ /de bzhin nyon mongs kyis
16b5(mdo 'grel): g.yogs pa'i/ /chos kyi dbyings kyang mthong ma yin/ /chos dbyings gang phyir bdag ma yin/ /bud med ma yin skyes ma yin/ /gzung ba kun las rnam grol bas/ /ji ltar 'dzin par brtag par bya/ /mi gtsang mi rtag sdug bsngal zhes/ /bya ba gsum pos sems sbyong byed//
16b6(mdo 'grel): stong pa nyid ni stong pa'i mdo/ /rgyal bas ji skad gsungs pa ste/ /de dag kun gyis nyon mongs ldog /khams de nyams par byed ma yin/ /mchog tu sems zhi sbyong byed pa'i/ /chos ni rang bzhin med pa yin/ /ji ltar ri bong mgo bo'i rwa/ /brtags pa nyid de med pa ltar/ /de
16b7(mdo 'grel): bzhin chos rnams thams cad kyang/ /brtags pa nyid de yod ma yin/ /phra rab rdul gyis ngo bo yis/ /glang gi rwa yang dmigs ma yin/ /ji ltar sngon bzhin byis de bzhin/ /de la ji zhig brtag par bya/ /brten nas 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang/ /brten nas 'gag par 'gyur ba dang/
17a1(mdo 'grel): gnas ba dag kyang yod min na/ /byis pa ji ltar rtog par byed/ /chos dbyings rang bzhin nam mkha' yi/ /khams ltar rgyu med rkyen med de/ /skye dang rga dang gnas pa dang/ /'jig pa med pa 'dus ma byas/ /sangs rgyas chos dbyer med pa dang/ /de rigs de bzhin thob
17a2(mdo 'grel): pa dang/ /brdzun med bslu med 'tshe med pas/ /gdod nas rang bzhin zhi nyid do/ /gang phyir de ni rgya mtsho ltar/ /sgra dang dpe dang blo rnams kyis/ /gting dang pha rol mi rnyed pa/ /de phyir rab tu zab ba nyid/ /chos kyi dbyings la dbyer med phyir/ /lta ba tha dad rung ma yin/ /'on kyang blo yi
17a3(mdo 'grel): byed brag gis/ /lta ba tha dad cung zad brjod/ /dbu ma nyid du smra ba rnams/ /de don bden pa gnyis su 'dod/ /kun rdzob dang ni don dam mo/ /bden gnyis rnam dbye shes pa dag /thub pa'i bka' la mi rmongs te/ /de dag ma lus tshogs bsags nas/ /phun tshogs pha rol 'gro
17a4(mdo 'grel): ba nyid/ /bdag dang bdag gi rtag chad dang/ /nyon mongs rnams byang rgyu 'bras dang/ /gzung dang 'dzin par gang spros pa/ /'di ni kun rdzob bden pa'o/ /stong nyid bdag med zhi ba gang/ /spros pa rnams kyi ma gos pa/ /tha dad don min rnams mi rtog /'di ni don dam bden pa'o//
17a5(mdo 'grel): yang dag yang dag ma yin dang/ rnams grangs rnam grangs ma yin pas/ /de gnyis so sor dbye ba byas/ /gtags tsam snang grags dngos po dang/ /tha snyad 'khrul ba sgyu ma dang/ /kun rdzob nyid ni rnams grangs so/ /stong pa nyid dang yang dag mdza' / /mtshan ma med dang don
17a6(mdo 'grel): dam dang/ /chos kyi dbyings ni rnam grangs so/ /gang phyir sgrib pa kun rdzob ste/ /'gyur ba med phyir don dam mo/ /yang dag yang dag ma yin pa'i/ /shes pa gnyis phyir bden pa gnyis/ /yang dag shes pa med ce na/ /bden te tha snyad tsam du yod/ /de nyid tshol la thog mar ni/ /thams
17a7(mdo 'grel): cad yod ces brjod par bya/ /don dam rtogs shing chags pa med/ /phyis ni rnam par dben don nyid/ /bden gnyis gcig dang tha dad min/ /nyes pa bzhi bzhi gsungs phyir ro/ /gcig dang tha dad gang rtog pa/ /de ni tshul min zhugs pa yin/ /dngos por khas len yod
17b1(mdo 'grel): na ni/ /'dod chags zhe sdang mi bzod 'byung/ /lta ba ma rungs yongs su 'dzin/ /de las byung ba'i rtsod par 'gyur/ /dmigs pa'i 'du shes can la ni/ /thos pa med cing mngon rtogs med/ /rjes mthun bzod pa'ang yod min na/ /mya ngan 'das pa'ang smos ci dgos/ /stong pa nyid la lta
17b2(mdo 'grel): nyes na/ /shes rab chung ldan 'phung bar 'gyur/ /ji ltar sprul la gzung nyes dang/ /rig sngags log par bsgrubs pa bzhin/ /rgyal ba kun gyis stong nyid ni/ /lta kun nges par 'byin par gsungs/ /gang dag stong pa nyid lta ba/ /de dag bsgrub tu med par gsungs/ /gang dag rang  
17b3(mdo 'grel): dngos gzhan dngos kyi/ /dngos dang dngos med nyid mthong ba/ /de dag sangs rgyas bstan pa la/ /yang dag mthong ba ma yin no/ /med pa yod pa'i zlas drangs te/ /yod pa'ang zhed pa'i zlas? drangs pas/ /de phyir med par brjod mi bya/ /yod pa nyid duAng mi brtag go /yod pa pa ni
17b4(mdo 'grel): bde 'gror 'gro/ /med pa pa ni ngan 'gror 'gro/ /yang dag ji bzhin yongs shes phyir/ /gnyis la mi brten thar bar 'gyur/ /tshul gnyis shing rta zhon nas su/ /rigs pa'i sub skyobs 'jug byed pa/ /de dag de phyir ji bzhin don/ /theg pa chen po ba nyid 'thob/ /gzugs sogs
17b5(mdo 'grel): ji ltar snang ba nas/ /bde gshegs bar gyi chos rnams kun/ /ri bong ba lang rwa yi de dpes/ /dbu ma nyid du goms bar bya/ /yod min med min yod med min/ /gnyis min bdag nyid du yang med/ /mdza' bzhi yang ni nges grol bas/ /de nyid dbu mar mkhas rnams bzhed/ /dbu ma
17b6(mdo 'grel): mthar las rnam grol na/ /mdza' dang bral phyir dbu ma'ang med/ /mdza' dbus med par gang lta ba/ /de yi yang dag lta ba ste/ /bla na med pa'i lta ba yin/ /blo ldan rnams kyis rtag tu bsgom/ /gang zhig lta ba der zhugs pa/ /des ni thams cad mkhyen pa thob/ /rnam rig tsam du smra
17b7(mdo 'grel): ba rnams/ /ngo bo nyid ni gsum du 'dod/ /kun brtags gzhan dbang yongs grub po/ /rtag dang rgyu las skye ba dang/ /mi 'gyur phyir na go rim bzhin/ /rnam par rtog pa gang gang gis/ /dngos po gang gang rnam brtags pa/ /de nyid kun tu rtags pa yi/ /ngo bo nyid de de med do/ /gzhan gyi dbang gang
18a1(mdo 'grel): bo nyid/ /rnam rtog yin te rkyen las byung/ /grub ni de la snga ma po/ /rtag tu med par gyur pa gang/ /yod dang med pa'i mdza' gnyis kyis/ /de phyir de nyid gzhan dbang las/ /gzhan min gzhan ma yin pa'ang min/ /mi rtag la sogs bzhin du brjod/ /chu
18a2(mdo 'grel): shel bai DUrya yi dpes/ /ngo bo nyid gsum shes par bya/ /bdag dang chos su brtags pa dang/ /rnam par dag dang ma dag dang/ /'gyur med phyin ci ma log pa/ /rim bzhin re re 'ang gnyis gnyis so/ /blo gros bzang po thams cad ni/ /nang sems pa la brtson pa yin//
18a3(mdo 'grel): gzung dang 'dzin pa las grol ba'i/ /rnam shes dam pa'i don du yod/ /chos rnams gang yang skye ba dang/ /'gag pa cung zad yod min te/ /shes pa 'ba' zhig kho na ni/ /skye ba dang ni 'gag bar 'gyur/ /yod min chos rnams de dag snang/ /bem po las min
18a4(mdo 'grel): gzhan las min/ /med pa las min nyes gnyis phyir/ /de phyir shes pa'i bdag nyid yod/ /rnam shes bem po'i rang bzhin las/ /bzlog par rab tu skye bar 'gyur/ khem min rang bzhin gang yin pa/ /de 'dir bdag nyid rig par 'dod/ /nam mkha' sa rlung nyi ma
18a5(mdo 'grel): dang/ rgya mtsho phyogs dang 'bab chu ni/ /nang gi shes pa yang dag gi /cha yin phyi rol ltar snang ngo/ /gsal ba'i rang bzhin du snang bas/ /de dag 'brel ba lkog gyur min/ /gang dang 'brel bas gang rig pa/ /de yis rig bya de rig 'gyur/ /ral gri'i so
18a6(mdo 'grel): dang sor rtse bzhin/ /blo yis rang 'dzin dor zhe na/ /rang nyid snang ba dor min par/ /dgongs pa nges par 'brel las gsungs/ /de phyir blo yi mtshan nyid ni/ /rang rig par ni grub pa yin/ /de nyid rtogs par dka' bas na/ /'di yi ngo bo spyad mi nus/ /rang rig de
18a7(mdo 'grel): yang phra ba'i phyir/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis phra bar gzigs/ /rang la gnas kyang bdag 'dra bas/ /rmongs pa'i phyir na mthong ba med/ /gsal dang blo ni bdag nyid kyi/ /'brel pa yod phyir blo tsam yin/ /shes pa'i rang bzhin bden pa ste/ /rnam pa
18b1(mdo 'grel): brdzun zhing 'khrul pa yin/ /sems ni rnam par bslang ba'i phyir/ /gcig nyid gnyis su snang ba yin/ /gzung dang 'dzin pa'i dbye ba las/ /shin tu mkhas pa cis ma yin/ /gzung ba'i rnam pa mi g.yo phyir/ /phyi rol lta bur snang ba yin/ /'dzin pa'i rnam par
18b2(mdo 'grel): rab g.yo bas/ /nang lta bur ni snang ba yin/ /mtshan ma de ni spangs nas su/ /ye shes nam mkha' lta bur bsgom/ /sems kyi rang bzhin zag pa med/ /zag bcas sa bon ma zad bar/ /kun gzhig gnas skabs de bdag nyid/ /zad nas zag pa med pa'i dbyings/ /rnam par grol ba'i sku
18b3(mdo 'grel): dang ni/ /rtag tu nyi zer nyi ma bzhin/ /sangs rgyas chos rnams gnas yin pas/ /skyob pa rnams kyis chos sku'o/ /nyan thos theg par zhugs pa rnams/ /bdag dang bdag gi dben pa yi/ /phung po khams dang skye mched dang/ /bzhi lnga 'am dus ni gsum yang rung/ /yod pa thams cad gzung
18b4(mdo 'grel): bya yin/ /dmigs dang bcas bas 'dzin par byed/ /de gnyis dam pa'i don du 'dod/ /bden pa mthong dang goms pa las/ /nyon mongs spangs ba zhes bshad pa/ /bden pa dag ni rnam bzhi ste/ /sdug bsngal de bzhin kun 'byung dang/ /'gog pa lam ste de lta na/ /de dag ji ltar mngon
18b5(mdo 'grel): rtogs rim/ /sdug bsngal nyer len phung po'o/ /kun 'byung las dang nyon mongs te/ /'gog pa mya ngan 'das pa gnyis/ /lam ni phyogs mthun sum cu bdun/ /tshul gnas thos dang sam ldan pa/ /bsgoms pa la ni rab tu sbyor/ /dge sbyong tshul ni dri med lam/ /'bras bu 'dus byas
18b6(mdo 'grel): 'dus ma byas/ /de dag brgyad cu rtsa dgu'o/ /grol lam zad pa rnams dang bcas/ /'bras bu bzhi rnams bzhag pa ni/ /rgyu lnga dag ni srid phyir ro/ /nyan thos rnam bzhi sbrul pa dang/ /rdzogs pa'i byang chub 'gyur ba dang/ /zhi bgrod grub mdza' 'dzin pa'o/ /de ni gnyis bzhi bco brgyad de//
18b7(mdo 'grel): gnyis ni bye brag smra ba dang/ /de bzhin mdo sde smra ba'o/ /rnam pa med pa'i shes pa yis/ /gzugs la sogs pa'i don rigs 'dod/ /de ni bye brag smra ba yin/ /gang zhig don gyis phan btags pa'i/ /gzugs brnyan rnams la nyams myong bas/ /don rig 'dod pa mdo sde pa'o//
19a1(mdo 'grel): bzhi ni dge 'dun phal chen pa/ /thams cad yod smra gnas brtan pa/ /mang pos bkur ba'o bco brgyad ni/ /shar dang nub dang gangs rir gnas/ /'jig rten 'das bar smra ba'i sde/ /btags bar smra ba'i sde pha dang/ /lnga tshan dge 'dun phal chen pa/ /gzhi kun
19a2(mdo 'grel): yod smra 'od srungs te/ /sa ston sde dang chos srung ste/ /mang thos gos dmar slob ma dang/ /rnam par phye ste smra ba'i sde/ /thams cad yod par smra ba yin/ /rgyal byed tshal gnas 'jigs med gnas/ /gtsug lag khang chen gnas brtan pa/ /sar sgrogs ris dang spung ba pa/ /gnas ma bu yi
19a3(mdo 'grel): sde pa ni/ /kun gyis bkur ba rnam pa gsum/ /yul don slob dpon bye brag gis/ /tha dad rnam pa bco brgyad do/ /rang rgyal byang chub don gnyer bas/ /gzung ba'i rtog pa spangs phyir dang/ /'dzin pa ma spangs phyir na de/ /rten gyis bse ru lta bu'i lam/ /bskal pa brgya yi mthar thug
19a4(mdo 'grel): par/ /bsgoms pas byang chub reg par 'gyur/ /de ni rten cing 'brel 'byung ba/ /yan lag bcu gnyis cha gsum mo/ /sngon dang phyi mthar gnyis gnyis dang/ /bar du brgyad yongs rdzogs ldan la/ /ma rig nyon mongs sngon gnas skabs/ /'du byed dag ni sngon las kyi/ /rnam shes mtshams
19a5(mdo 'grel): sbyor phung po yin/ /ming dang gzugs ni de man chad/ /skye mched drug dod tshun chad do/ /de ni gsum 'dus tshun chad do/ /reg pa bde sdug la sogs kyi/ /rgyu shes nus pa tshun chad do/ /tshor 'khrig tshun chad sred pa ni/ /longs spyod 'khrig pa chags bcas kyi/ /nye bar len pa longs
19a6(mdo 'grel): spyod rnams/ /thob par bya phyir yongs rgyug pa'i/ /de srid 'bras bu 'byung 'gyur ba'i/ /las de nyid ni srid pa yin/ /nying mtshams sbyor ba skye ba yin/ /tshor ba'i bar ni rga shi yin/ /'di ni gnas skabs par 'dod do/ /gtso bo'i phyir na yan lag bsgrags/ /sngon dang phyi mdza' 
19a7(mdo 'grel): bar dag la/ /rmongs pa rnam par bzlog phyir ro/ /nyon mongs gsum mo las gnyis so/ /bzhi bdun de bzhin 'bras bu yin/ /gnyis kyi rgyu 'bras mdor bsdus pa/ /bar ma'i rjes su dpag pa las/ /'dir ni 'byung ba rgyu yin te/ /byung ba 'bras bu nyid du 'dod/ /yan lag bcu
19b1(mdo 'grel): gnyis de dag las/ /rgyu ni rnam lnga 'bras bu bdun/ /'phen par byed dang 'phangs pa dang/ /mngon par 'grub byed grub pa dang/ /nyes dmigs kyis ni yan lag ste/ /gsum bzhi gsum gcig gcig rim bzhin/ /'du byed sdug bsngal 'gyur ba yi/ /sdug bsngal nyid ni rim bzhin du/ /lnga
19b2(mdo 'grel): dang gnyis dang lnga yin no/ /khams gsum du ni rim bzhin du/ /bcu gnyis bcu gcig bcu yis 'jug/ rdzus skyes yan lag bcu gcig gis/ /mngal dang sgong skyes bcu gnyis kyis/ /drod gsher las skyes ci rigs 'jug /de bzhin 'gro ba lnga la sbyar/ /gsum po dag las gnyis 'byung
19b3(mdo 'grel): ste/ /gnyis las bdun 'byung bdun las kyang/ /gsum 'byung srid pa'i 'khor lo de/ /nyid ni yang dang yang du 'khor/ /'khor ba'i ngo bo rnam pa dang/ /gang zhig gang du gang gis dang/ /ji ltar ji srid nyes dmigs ni/ /mdza' yas tshogs kyis rab tu 'jug /brtsam par bya zhing
19b4(mdo 'grel): 'byung bar bya/ /sangs rgyas bstan la 'jug par bya/ /'dam bu'i khyim la glang chen bzhin/ /'chi bdag sde ni gzhom par bya/ /gang zhig rab tu bag yod par/ /chos 'dul 'di la spyod gyur pa/ /skye ba'i 'khor ba rab spangs nas/ /sdug bsngal tha mar byed par 'gyur/ /mya
19b5(mdo 'grel): ngan gang las 'da' ba dang/ /gang zhig gang gis gang gi tshe/ /gang du gang phyir ji lta bur/ /ji srid ngo bo rnam pa dang/ thob pa dbye ba phrin las dang/ /yon tan tshogs kyis ldog pa'o/ /mu stegs pa ni rnam pa gnyis/ /sprul pa pa dang rang rgyud pa/ /de yang skyes thob sbyor byung ngo//
19b6(mdo 'grel): skyes thob rigs chad log sred can/ /sbyor byung bsam gtan rtog ge pa/ /bsam gtan pa ni mngon shes mthus/ /lta ba drug cu gnyis su rtog /rtag par smra ba rnam bzhi dang/ /kha gcig rtag par smra pa bzhi/ /mdza' yod sogs bzhi mi spong bzhi/ /rgyu med gnyis ni sngon mthar
19b7(mdo 'grel): rtog /'du shes mod smra bcu drug dang/ /med smra brgyad dang de bzhin du/ /yod min med min smra ba brgyad/ /chang smra bdun dang tshe 'di la/ /mya ngan 'da' bar smra ba lnga/ /phyi ma'i mthar rtog lta ba'o/ /rtog ge pa ni grangs can sogs/ /tshad mas grub mdza' 'dzin pa'o/ /grangs can
20a1(mdo 'grel): yon tan gsum du brjod/ /snying stob rdul dang mun pa'o/ /rangs dang mgu dang kun dga' dang/ /bde dang zhi ba'i sems nyid dag/ res 'ga' yang ni snang 'gyur ba/ /de dag snying stobs yon tan no/ /mi dga' ba dang yongs gsungs dang/ /mya ngan 'dod dang mi
20a2(mdo 'grel): bzod dag /gang du sna ba'i gtan tshigs kyis/ /de dag rdul gyi rtags su 'dod/ /rmongs dang de bzhin gti mug dang/ /bag med gnyid dang g.yel ba dang/ /lan 'ga' yang ni snang gyur pa/ /de dag mun pa'i yon tan no/ /yon tan gsum gyi rang bzhin mchog /mthong ba'i lam du 'gyur ma
20a3(mdo 'grel): yin/ /mthong ba'i lam du gang gyur pa/ /sgyu ma bzhin du shin tu gso ba/ /rang bzhin las ni chen po ste/ /de las nga rgyal rnam gsum 'byung/ /de las dbang po bcu gcig dang/ /de tsam lnga'o de lnga las/ /'byung ba lnga skye nyi shu bzhi/ /gtso bo nyid dang rnam 'gyur ro/ /de dag sems pa yod
20a4(mdo 'grel): ma yin/ /skyes bu kun rig sems pa can/ /de nyid nyi shu lnga shes na/ /ral pa'am spyi po 'am gtsug bud kyis/ /bsti nas gang du dga' ba der/ /grol 'gyur 'di la the tshom med/ /bye brag pa ni drug du 'dod/ /rdzas dang yon tan las dang spyi/ /bye brag 'du ba rnam pa drug /rdzas dgu yon
20a5(mdo 'grel): tan nyi shu bzhi/ /las lnga spyi gnyis bye brag gnyis/ /de bzhin 'du ba'ang rnam gnyis te/ /de nyid drug shes rig pa'i mchog /rig byed kun gyi pha rol phyin/ /gcer bu ba rnams don dgu smra/ /srog dang zag pa sdom pa dang/ /nges par rga dang 'chi ba dang/ /las dang sdig dang bsod nams dang//
20a6(mdo 'grel): thar pa zhes bya don dgu po/ /gang gis mthong de rnam par dag /rigs pa can don bcu drug 'dor/ /tshad ma gzhal bya the tshom dang/ /dgos pa dpe dang grub mdza' dang/ /cha shas rtog ge gtan la dbab/ /rtsod dang brjod dang rgol ba dang/ /rgyu ltar snang ba tshig dor dang/ /lhag tshod chang ba'i gnas
20a7(mdo 'grel): rnams te/ /bcu drug gis ni nges par 'byung/ /dpyod pa pa ni don bzhir brjod/ /sa dang chu dang me dang rlung/ /de dag 'dus ma byas pa ste/ /rtag tu skye 'gag med par gnas/ /de bas las 'bras yod ma yin/ /sngon dang phyi mdza' de bzhin med/ /gang zhig de ltar rnam spyod pa/ /mthong ba tsam gyis
20b1(mdo 'grel): rnam grol 'gyur/ /khyab 'jug byed rgyur smra ba rnams/ /nyi ma'i nang na bdag khyab 'jug /skar nang 'od gnas zla ba yin/ /rlung nang nga ni 'od zer can/ /snang ba can na nyi ma yin/ /rig byed nang na snyan tshig dang/ /lha nang nga ni brgya byin te/ /dbang po'i nang na yid yin no/ /'byung ba'i nang nas yin zhing/ /nga ni bde
20b2(mdo 'grel): byed drag po'ang yin/ /srin po gnod sbyin nang nor bdag nor lha'i nang na me lha nga/ /ri bo'i nang nang ri rab/ /nga ni yi ge'i nang na a/ /nya dang dul sbal phag dang ni/ /mi yi sang ge mi'u thung dang/ /dga' byed rA ma Na nag pa/ /sangs rgyas kar ki ke dang bcu/ /gang gis khyab
20b3(mdo 'grel): 'jug yon tan rnams/ /rtag tu bsgoms na bde thob 'gyur/ dbang phyug byed rgyud 'dod pa rnams/ /'gro ba 'di dag thams cad kyi/ /byed pa po ni dbang phyug yin/ /de ni yon tan brgyad dang ldan/ /rab phra yang ba mchod par 'os/ /bdag por gyur dang dbang du gyur/ /gar yang phyin dang 'dod
20b4(mdo 'grel): dgur ldan/ /de bzhin dga' mgur gnas pa'o/ /lag pa dag dang rkang pa dang/ /mig dang gdong dang lus rnams kyis/ /mang po bskyed cing 'jig byed pas/ /des na phra bar brjod pa yin/ /mkha' dang rlung dang sa dang ni/ /chu dang me dag gnas byed cing/ /sdud pa dang ni rgyas byed pas/ /des
20b5(mdo 'grel): na yan bar brjod ba yin/ /'jig rten gsum na mchod gyur cing/ /gnas pa dag dang rgyu ba dang/ /'byung po kun gyis rjed bas na/ /des na mchod par 'os pa yin/ /'byung po kun la dbang byed cing/ /gnas pa dag dang rgyu ba dang/ /gang dang gang 'dod des byed pas/ /des na bdag por
20b6(mdo 'grel): gyur ces bya/ /bdag la rag las rang dbang can/ /'ga' la'ang 'jigs pa yod min te/ /thams cad dbang du gyur pas na/ /des na dbang du gyur ces bya/ /mtho ris ngan song kun khyab pas/ /des na gar yang phyin ces bya/ /snying stobs rdul dang mun pa gsum/ /de dag gang las
20b7(mdo 'grel): gnas gyur pa/ /mig 'byed tsam gyis byed 'gyur bas/ /des na 'dod dgur ldan zhes bya/ /thar pa 'am yang na lha 'i lus/ /gang du bdag nyid 'dod pa dag /thams cad 'dod pas thob 'gyur bas/ /des na dga' mgur gnas shes bya/ /gang zhig phra gyur cig pu skyes gnas 'dug /
21a1(mdo 'grel): de yis 'di kun skye zhing 'jig par byed/ /de ni dbang bdag mchog sbyin lha mchod bya/ /yon tan byed po shin tu zhi ba 'thob/ /skye ba po 'di shes pa yod min te/ /bdag gi bde sdug bdag la rang dbang med/ /dbang phyug gis btang yang na mtho ris
21a2(mdo 'grel): sam/ /g.yangs dag tu 'gro ba kho nar 'gyur/ /dbang phyug rdza mkhan lta bur sna tshogs 'di sprul byed por ma gyur na/ /ri rab 'di mi 'grub cing sa gzhi 'di min rgya mtsho 'ang ma yin te/ nyi zla skar ldan 'di ltar bkod pa 'di dag mig yul du mi 'gyur/ /yod pa'i phyir na
21a3(mdo 'grel): dbang phyug 'gro ba'i byed po yin zhes 'ga' zhig smra/ /phra zhing bsam gyis mi khyab rab srab byed ba kun rig kun byed pa/ /rnal 'byor goms pas thob pa blo can bsam gtan pa yi bsam gtan yul/ /nyi ma zla bas chu me rlung phyogs dang nam mkha' i lus can te/ /zhi
21a4(mdo 'grel): ba'i bde dga' 'dod pa rnams kyis dbang phyug rtag tu bsgom/ /dus la bltos par smra ba rnams/ /dngos kun dus kyis bsgyur ba ste/ /gang gi zhang pa nor lha dang/ /gang pha nor rgyal yin pa yi/ /'jigs med khro bo'ang bsad gyur pas/ /dus ni 'da' bar dka' ba yin//
21a5(mdo 'grel): 'byung ba rnams ni dus kyis 'byin/ /skye dgu rnams sdung dus kyis byed/ dus kyis gnyid log sang par byed/ /dus ni 'da' bar dka' ba yin/ /srung ba gsum rtsegs 'obs ni rgya mtsho dang/ /dmags mi srin po nor ni nor sbyin sbyor/ /gang gi bstan bcos pa sangs tshad mnyam
21a6(mdo 'grel): pa'i/ /sgra sgrogs bu de'ang dus kyi dbang gis nyams/ /ngo bo nyid rgyur smra dngos rnams/ /ngo bo nyid kyis 'grub par byed/ /mi yi dmar ba nyid dang ni/ /dam pa gzhan don byed nyid dang/ /dam pa min pa'i brtse min nyid/ /gsum po? ngo bo nyid kyis grub/ /tsher ma rno bar gyur pa su
21a7(mdo 'grel): yis byas/ /ri dags bya yi ri mo su yis byas/ /bu ram shing mngar nim pa kha bdag 'di dag thams cad ngo bo nyid kyis grub/ /nyi ma tsha zhing zla ba rab bsil dang/ /skye bo chags shing thub pa de min la/ /bde ba rab tshim sdug bsngal rab gdung pa/ /drug po 'di dag ngo bo nyid
21b1(mdo 'grel): kyis grub/ /gang dag rgyu med smra ba ni/ /thams cad rgyu la bltos? med par/ /dngos po rnams ni skye ba ste/ /nyi ma pad+ma'i ge sar sogs/ /sna tshogs gang gis byas pa yin/ /rma bya'i mdongs la sogs pa yang/ /sna tshogs gang gis sprul pa yin/ /ji ltar char rlung la sogs pa/ /glo bur 'byung phyir
21b2(mdo 'grel): rgyu med ltar/ /sdug bsngal la sogs rgyu med nyid/ /shin tu rgya chen rab zab la/ /sgying lug shin tu ma sbyangs pa/ /bdag gzhan smra dag gti mug gis/ /de ltar theg pa chen la smod/ /tshul khrims las ni nyams bla yi/ /lta las cis kyang ma yin te/ /tshul khrims kyis ni mtho ris
21b3(mdo 'grel): 'gro/ /lta bas go 'phangs mchog tu 'gyur/ /gti mug dbang gis bsgribs gyur te/ /gang zhig yang dag gegs byed pa/ /de la dge ba'i 'gro ba'ang med/ /thar pa med pa smos ci dgos/ /gnod pa'i sa bon gyur pa yis/ /mu stegs byed mang mthong nas ni/ /thar 'dod skye ba po rnams
21b4(mdo 'grel): la/ /snying rjer mi 'gyur su zhig yod/ /de phyir thar pa don gnyer rnams/ /chos kyi dbyings su blta bar gyis/ /chos kyi dbyings su lta ba'i glu slob dpon chen po dI ra baM ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi mkhan po de nyid dang/ /bod kyi lo tsA ba dge slong tshul
21b5(mdo 'grel): khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o// //*/ /rgya gar skad du/ e ka smri tyA pa de sha/ bod skad du/ dran pa gcig pa'i man ngag /bcom ldan 'das 'jig rten dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thams cad mkhyen la gus btud de/ /'phags pa klu sgrub phyag 'tshal nas//
21b6(mdo 'grel): a ba d+hU ti bdag gis ni/ /cig car 'jug pa'i man ngag bri/ /'dir byang chub sems dpa' sems dang po bskyed pa nas nye bar gzung ste dbang bskur chen po ma thob kyi bar de srid du de'i bya ba ni gnyis te/ /shes rab kyi bya ba dang/ /thabs kyi bya ba'o/ /de la shes rab ni
21b7(mdo 'grel): chos thams cad gdod ma nas ma skyes pa dang po nyid nas chos kyi dbyings nyid du shes pa'o/ /de'i bya ba ni las dang po ba de nyid nas ji srid dbang bskur ba ma thob kyi bar de srid du nyin mtshan dus rtag du de nyid bsgom pa'o/ /thabs ni sems can mi gtong ba'i byang  
22a1(mdo 'grel): chub kyi sems so/ /de'i bya ba ni lus dang ngag dang yid kyi bya ba thams cad sems can thams cad kyi ched ma yin pa ci yang med de/ dngos sam brgyud pas so/ /'dir yang sems can la dmigs pa dang/ dmigs pa med pa'i rim pa'o/ /de'i rim pa ni 'di yin te/ mi mkhas
22a2(mdo 'grel): pa rab rib can dang/ /mkhas pa rab rib dangs pa'o/ /gang gi tshe chos kyi sku mngon sum du mdzad phan chad shes rab mnga' ste/ ye shes nyid du gyur nas gnas so/ /shes rab kyi bya ba ni mi mnga' ste goms nas mthar phyin pa'i phyir ro/ /thabs de'i bya ba ni dmigs pa med pa rang gi ngang
22a3(mdo 'grel): gis lhun gyis grub pa dang/ 'bad pa dang rtsol ba med par 'byung ngo/ /byang chub sems dang las dang po pas ni gang zag gi bdag yod pas sems can zhes brtags shing/ /des sdug bsngal ba la snying rje bskyed do/ /de nas goms nas ni sems can zhes bya ba ni dang po
22a4(mdo 'grel): nyid nas med kyi/ glo bur du brtags par zad do/ /gzhan du na rten 'brel gyi phung po dang khams dang skye mched tsam zhig las gzhan 'di na ci yang med do snyam du rtogs pa dang/ yang 'di dag ni rang gi sems 'ba' zhig tu zad kyi gzhan 'di na ci yang med do snyam du rtogs nas/
22a5(mdo 'grel): nges sdug bsngal ba rnams la snying rje skye'o/ /gang gi tshe sangs rgyas kyi sa la ni dmigs pa'i yul med de/ 'phags pa rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa las ji skad du/ sangs rgyas bcom 
22a6(mdo 'grel): ldan 'das kyi ye shes kyis ci yang mi gzigs te/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ ye shes kyi yul
22a7(mdo 'grel): mi mnga' ba'i phyir ro zhes gsungs so/ /'o na dus de na ye shes yod dam med ce na/ /'phags pa klu sgrub mi bzhed de/ ji skad du/ sems ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyis/ /ma gzigs mi gzigs gzigs mi 'gyur/ /rang bzhin med pa'i rang bzhin la/ /ci lta bu zhig gzigs
22a8(mdo 'grel): par 'gyur/ zhes gsungs pa dang/ brgyud pa'i man ngag 'di yin no/ /dren gzhan gyi don las ma gtogs pa bya ba gzhan ci yang mi mnga' la/ 'di ltar gzhan gyi don ni 'dod par bya ba'i don gyi 'bras bu'i gtso bo yin te/ ji skad du/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal snga nas/ gzhan
22b1(mdo 'grel): don phun sum tshogs pa ni/ /'bras bu spyi'i gtso yin par 'dod/ /sangs rgyas nyid sogs de las gzhan/ /de dag don gyi 'bras bur 'dod/ /ces gsungs so/ /de kho na nyid la 'jug pa'i man ngag kyang blo la gnas par bya'o/ /tshul khrims rgyal bas bskul ba yis/ /'dir ni bsdus
22b2(mdo 'grel): nas bstan pa yin/ /rgyas par klu sgrub gdams ngag dang/ /theg chen mdo sde blta bar gyis/ /cig car 'jug pa'i man ngag /paN+Di ta dI baM ka ra sh+rI dz+nyA nas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //panDi ta de nyid dang lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o// // */ /rgya gar skad
22b3(mdo 'grel): du/ bo d+hi satwa karmA di manA ba tA ra de sha na/ bod skad du/ byang chub sems dpa' las dang po pa'i lam la 'jug pa bstan pa/ /bla ma dam pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /ngan 'gro 'khor ba 'joms pa dang/ /mngon mtho nges 'byung stsol mdzad pa/ /phyogs bcu'i dkon mchog
22b4(mdo 'grel): thams cad dang/ /dpal ldan bla ma'i zhabs phyag 'tshal/ /'di na gang dag rang bzhin gyis snying rje dang shes rab che ba theg pa chen po'i rigs can dang/ yang gang dag skye ba snga ma dag tu theg pa chen po la goms par byas pa'i skyes bu 'khor ba la yid legs bar byung ba/
22b5(mdo 'grel): 'chi ba rjes su dran pa/ phyi nang gi dngos po thams cad la zhen pa chung ba/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen dam pa zhig la theg pa chen po'i lam phyin ci ma log pa zhig thos par gyur na ci ma rung/ bdag gis dam pa zhig btsal bar bya'o snyam du sems pa des/ dge ba'i bshes
22b6(mdo 'grel): gnyen du rung ba'i bla ma btsal te/ /gzhan du bstan pa bzhin du gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba khyad par can dang/ 'gro ba mdza' yas yul du byas te/ bsam pa bzang po dang ldan pas bla na med pa'i byang chub chen por sems thun mong ma yin pa bskyed pa dang/ lhag pa'i
22b7(mdo 'grel): bsam pa bzang po dang ldan pas g.yo sgyu dang bral ba'i 'jug pa byang chub kyi sems chen po'i byang chub sems dpa' i tshul khrims kyi bslab pa gsum legs par blang par bya'o/ /de nas khyi dang gdol ba dang bran gyi 'du shes dang ldan pa/ g.yo sgyu dang bral ba'i byang
23a1(mdo 'grel): chub sems dpa' de tshogs kyi lam ma yin pas nyin dang mtshan du lus dang ngag dang yid kyi bya ba thams cad don med par mi 'gyur ro/ /'di ltar sems des zas kyi chod rig bar bya ba dang/ dbang po'i sgo? rnams bsngam pa dang/ kha na ma thob phra rab tsam
23a2(mdo 'grel): la yang 'jigs par lta bu dang/ nyin dang mtshan du rnal 'byor la brtson par bya'o/ /de nas dbugs phyi nang du rgyu ba yang gzhan gyi ngan du 'gyur bar 'dod pa nges tho rangs kyi thun las langs te/ bshad ba dang gcib dang ba la sogs pa'i spyod lam legs par byas nas
23a3(mdo 'grel): yul dbus dang yul mdza' khob kyi bye brag gis khrus byas la/ /'gro ba mdza' dag la dmigs te/ /tshang med pa bzhis byang chub tu sems bskyed la/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gzugs brnyan gyi spyan sngar byug ris legs par byas te me tog dri zhim po sil ma legs par gtor nas/
23a4(mdo 'grel): de dag gi spyan sngar pus mo gnyis sal gtsugs nas thal mo sbyar te/ phyog bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sangs rgyas thams cad dang chos thams cad dang/ theg pa chen po'i dge 'dun gyi spyan sngar lus kyi bkod pa grangs med cing brjod du med par sprul te/ de dag re re'i zhabs la
23a5(mdo 'grel): legs par phyag bya'o/ /de dag la zang zing gi mchod pa tshad med pa rgya che ba dpag tu med pas mnyes par bya'o/ /de nas lus re re la mgo bo brjod du med pa/ mgo bo re re la lce brjod du med pa sprul te/ bdag dang gzhan gyi sdig pa ma lus par bshags par bya'o/ /bdag dang
23a6(mdo 'grel): gzhan gyi dge pa la rjes su yi rang bar bya'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas ring po ma lon pa rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bskul ma gdab par bya'o/ /gang dag chos kyi 'khor lo bskor nas che'i 'du byed gtong ba de dag la
